City News 146

Xinhua Bank Establishes Office. Xinhua Bank, to facilitate its customers in the French Concession, has established a fourth office at the intersection of Hualong Road and Avenue Joffre. It officially opened yesterday. The office director is Mr. He Yangxian, the bank's assistant manager.

China National Products Company Children's Amusement Market First Day. The Children's Amusement Market, sponsored by the China National Products Company (Nanjing Road Continental Department Store), has opened. Yesterday was the first day, and the guests were all children, who were extremely crowded. The mayor personally hosted them, offering refreshments. The children were very satisfied. The internal facilities included Zhongshan Park, an art room, a library, an animal courtyard, a reception room, a clubhouse, the mayor's office, a large kitchen, a bedroom, etc. The mayor was Mr. Lin Zhifu, the son of Mr. Lin Kanghou. The vice mayors were Miss Huang Suhui, the daughter of Mr. Huang Renzhi, and Miss Pan Shiwei, the daughter of Mr. Pan Yangyao. For every purchase of small items totaling 5 jiao, a ticket can be drawn to exchange for exquisite gifts that children love. The company's spring sale is today, the last day. Those who want to obtain cheap goods can go there immediately. The opportunity will not come again.

National Product Straws to be Released. Most of the straws used for cold drinks in summer are imported. The outflow of rights and interests each year is quite considerable. Recently, Mr. Du Zhaotang, a wealthy Guangdong businessman in Shanghai, based on his years of experience in operating canned food in Shanghai and in view of the aforementioned reasons, has used scientific methods to produce a national product straw to meet market demand. It is said that the straw is strong, durable, and priced cheaper than imported goods. Once the installation is completed, it will begin to be released. The general manager's office is located in the Zhaohua Company at number 88, Quanji An Road. Major companies, food stores, etc., all have sales agents.

Dehe Restaurant Officially Opens. Dehe Restaurant, a Chinese and Western cuisine restaurant at the intersection of Wuma Road and Shandong Road, officially opened yesterday. Business was booming, and the dishes were well-cooked and suitable. The prices were extremely low. Last night, manager Zhou Zijin invited people from all walks of life to a banquet. Many people attended.

Shenchang Watch Company Opens. The Shenchang Watch Company's new main store in the Paobujichang, Nanjing Road of this city. It is said that the company is the hub of Shenchang's branches in all ports, with strong capital and a wide variety of goods. It is scheduled to open tomorrow and will offer special cheap goods as a sacrifice for the opening celebration. There will be a very grand occasion at that time.

Mi Ye & Co. Hires Chinese Manager. The famous German company Mi Ye & Co., which has always managed famous German machines and fabrics, has now hired Mr. Zhao Xianglin as the Chinese manager of the machinery department. Mr. Zhao has been well-known in the electrical industry for a long time, has a wide circle of friends, and is very experienced in machinery. It is expected that business will flourish in the future. The company's business department is located at number 16, Guangdong Road.

Publishing Industry 148

Briand Special Price Sale. Since its opening last year, the Peiping Renwen Bookstore has been actively operating. In just a few months, it has published more than a dozen famous books. The Origins of Chinese New Literature by Zhou Zuoren, the Modern Prose Collection edited by Shen Qiguang, and Twelve Lectures on Japanese Grammar written by Zhang Wojun have already been adopted as textbooks by several schools, so sales are very brisk. The recently published Briand was written by French man Valentien Thompson and translated by Changde Zhou Jiu'an. The content is rich, and the translation is clear and smooth. All of Briand's words and deeds are recorded in detail. It is a must-have book for those who are concerned about politics and diplomacy. The hardback book, printed on high-quality Dowling paper, is priced at 2.6 yuan.

Newsprint edition, priced at 2 yuan, is now discounted by 30% to benefit readers. It is reported that the books have already arrived in Shanghai and are being sold on consignment by Peiwenbao Bookstore on the west end of Guangxi Road, Sanma Road, and major bookstores on Sima Road.

Reader's Advisor

Discussion on "Can one go back to the countryside?" 152

丨 Mr. You Huaigao of the Ziyou Farm on Connaught Road, Shanghai

Letter in response to Mr. Xiongsheng of this column丨

The prerequisites for going to the countryside: (1) Do you love the countryside? (2) Do you sincerely love the farmers in your village? (3) Can you resolutely endure hardship to make a living in the countryside? The advantages of the countryside are: (1) closeness to nature, without the pollution of the city; (2) honest people, without the deception of the city; (3) freedom of life, without the interference of the city. The hardships of the countryside are: (1) lack of support, unable to obtain material enjoyment; (2) people who have lived in the city for a long time may feel lonely and bored. However, I feel that in this time of national crisis, seeing the drunken, dreamlike lives in the cities, it is better to find a quiet and lovely village to seek a new path. Within my capabilities, I can spend ten years building a new-style Peach Blossom Spring in my mind. The city lacks food and materials, which the countryside can provide. Judging from the current situation in our country, farmers who know a few characters are truly as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns. Therefore, the countryside lacks talent. According to Mr. Xiongsheng, a talent who is an unemployed person with no place to be in the city is a leader who stands out from the crowd in the countryside. How can you say, "I don't have the guts to break the law, and I don't have the courage to commit suicide"? I absolutely advocate saving the country through rural education. The land of the Shanghai concessions is very limited and can never accommodate tens of thousands of returned students from various countries and graduates from universities and middle schools. The only way out for the intellectual class is to undertake the education and revitalization of the countryside. The life of a family of three in the countryside requires about four mu of farmland, or at least two mu near the city, but it must be cultivated by oneself with the cooperation of the wife to succeed. Given that Mr. Xiongsheng can only write and cannot plow, it is no wonder that he sighs and feels helpless. But I have a method to design for Mr. Xiongsheng: The first step is to teach: raise one or two hundred yuan (at least one hundred yuan) from relatives and friends. It is best to return to your hometown during this warm spring season, because dialect is extremely important. Find a village with relatively abundant production, a good livelihood, and a slightly larger population. Live in this village and stay for a few days to investigate the number of school-age children. If you rent two small houses from the villagers, the rent will be no more than ten yuan per year. One room can be used as a classroom, and the other as a reception room and bedroom. You can board with neighbors for three meals a day. This will save countless troubles and useful time for studying and reading. Subscribe to a daily newspaper and explain it to the villagers in your spare time. (When you have the strength in the future, you can buy a radio. I predict that the government will definitely use broadcasting to educate farmers in the future, because this is a powerful tool for universal education.) Mr. Xiongsheng's clothes can be Zhongshan suits made of cloth in spring, summer, and autumn, and cloth robes in winter. According to this plan, Mr. Xiongsheng's clothing, food, housing, daily life, and classroom problems can all be solved in a very economical way. Seventy percent of the education funding is for teachers' salaries, and miscellaneous expenses are even cheaper in the countryside. As for Mr. Xiongsheng's life, it can be done in the following ways: (1) Collect a small amount of tuition, one yuan per class, set it appropriately, and do not force it; (2) It is best to order each student to pay one chicken or one duck, or thirty eggs to the school at the end of each year. This chicken can be called the "reading chicken," which is not difficult for farmers, but it is an income for the school. I advocate having a sacrificial heart in the first year, and always spreading goodwill in the village to gain the trust of the farmers. After three or four years, when the students grow up, they will be your followers. The second step is to help farmers organize cooperatives. If it can be a little successful, banks in Shanghai and farmers' banks can provide loans. This is a very important matter. If this matter can be accomplished, your foundation will be very solid. The third step is to practice medicine and sell medicine. The most prevalent diseases in the countryside are autumn dysentery and red eyes. There are effective medicines that can cure these, such as quinine. However, only sell effective medicines and never be greedy and harm people's lives. This is also a source of income. The fourth step is that after the above three things are accomplished, your position will increase day by day, and the number of students will also increase day by day. You will be a leader in the village, and then you can carry out village governance work. But at the same time, you can communicate with various academic institutions, provincial construction institutions, agricultural schools, etc. to solve difficult problems. At the same time, you can also contact nearby villages or towns. If you feel that one person is not enough, you can invite one confidant to handle it together. Reporter's note: Mr. You Huaihuang is an enthusiastic advocate of saving the country through rural education. He has a lot of research on rural education and is a practitioner. I have received a letter in which he answers the letter from Mr. Xiongsheng in yesterday's column, "Can one go back to the countryside?" His kindness is admirable! In addition to publishing the original letter, readers are welcome to send letters to discuss any opinions.

Education News 153

Important News

Record of the Third Day of the Astronomy and Mathematics Discussion Meeting 154

Passed more than 500 astronomical translations

Encourage various bookstores to publish mathematics series

Reward the compilation of university physics textbooks

丨The Central Government held a public banquet for all members in the evening丨

(Nanjing, 4th) At the Astronomy and Mathematics Discussion Meeting of the Ministry of Education, the members of the astronomy group were eager to continue the discussion on the morning of the 4th, so they did not participate in the tour. They held a group meeting at 8 o'clock. Nine people attended, chaired by Zhang Yuzhe. More than 200 astronomical translations were passed. Other group members all toured scenic spots. In the afternoon at 2 o'clock, the astronomy group continued the meeting, chaired by Zhang Yun. More than 300 astronomical translations were passed. In the past three days, more than 1,000 have been passed. There are still more than 400 left, and it was decided to complete the discussion by the morning of the 5th. The mathematics group continued the discussion at 2 o'clock in the afternoon, chaired by Feng Zugou. The minimum required courses were passed, and about 50 kinds of reference books were examined. It was also resolved to ask the Ministry of Education and the National Compilation and Translation Bureau to jointly compile a series of mathematics books with professors, researchers, and researchers from various universities, and to encourage various bookstores to publish mathematics series as much as possible. The physics group, chaired by Hu Gangfu, resolved: 1. This discussion meeting will entrust the Physics Society to solicit opinions from various academic institutions to select excellent physics textbooks and important reference books for universities and middle schools, add detailed discussions, and submit them to the National Compilation and Translation Bureau. 2. It is recommended that the National Compilation and Translation Bureau effectively reward the compilation and translation of physics textbooks and reference books for all grades of universities. At 6:30 in the evening, the Central Government held a public banquet for all members at the Lizhi Society. The guests and hosts toasted each other happily.

Zhejiang Provincial Scout Grand Review 155

Dai Jitao attended and gave instructions

The Second Zhejiang Provincial Scout Grand Review and Grand Camp was held at 9:00 am on April 4th at the Zhejiang Provincial Stadium in Hangzhou. A total of 39 scout groups from various counties participated in the province, with 2,670 people. The weather was clear and sunny that day. The scouts began to prepare at 7:00 am. Later, inspectors Dai Jitao, Chen Bulei, Xu Shaodi, etc. arrived. The scouts from each group took the field and marched around for a week. Then the ceremony was held. After the chairman Xu Shaodi reported, the scouts performed a parade. Under the leadership of the commander-in-chief Hu Liren, the inspectors inspected the basic movements. Then the march was held. The scouts from each group passed the reviewing stand one by one for inspection. The military band also joined in. The scouts moved quickly and were in excellent spirits. Then they stood in front of the stage in order to listen to the instructions. Finally, they sang the Boy Scout Song, cheered, and the ceremony was completed with a photo.

Instructions: First, Dai Chuanxian, vice president of the General Association of Boy Scouts of China, encouraged the scouts not to forget the three oaths and to use them as the foundation. Then, Xue Yuanlong, representative of the Preparatory Office of the Boy Scout General Association, Zheng Yi, representative of the Provincial Party Department, Chen Bulei, representative of the Provincial Government, and others all gave instructions.

Course competition: The order of the afternoon course competition was originally set as (1) Old Lyric Rules, with a total of 38 groups participating, (2) Knotting, with a total of 38 groups, (3) Fire Making, with a total of 36 groups, (4) Rescue, with a total of 23 groups, (5) Semaphore, A, Pen-exhausted Semaphore, with a total of 6 groups, B, Sound Transmission Semaphore, with a total of 4 groups, C, English Semaphore, with a total of 18 groups, D, Chinese Semaphore, with a total of 2 groups, (6) Observation, with a total of 34 groups, (7) Measurement, with a total of 22 groups, (8) Shooting, with a total of 30 groups, (9) Engineering, A, Bridge Building, with a total of 14 groups, B, Building a Lookout Tower, with a total of 9 groups, (10) Bicycle Communication, A, Men's Group, with a total of 21 groups, Women's Group, with a total of 2 groups. Later, due to lack of time, only knotting, fire making, and observation were held. It was decided to continue the competition tomorrow.

The Ministry of Education orders all schools to implement the new system of weights and measures 156

(Nanjing, 4th) After the government issued an order to switch to the new system of weights and measures, it ordered the use of the new system of market feet for arithmetic and drawing in various schools. However, the new system of English feet is still used in various schools, and it has not yet been promoted. The Shanghai Baoguan Weights and Measures Manufacturing Factory specially manufactured some standard market feet and presented them to the Ministry of Industry, which transferred them to the Ministry of Education for distribution to various science universities for procurement as drawing rulers, in order to prevent foreign goods and benefit the weights and measures policy. The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 4th for all schools to follow and purchase.

Shandong University Science Museum Opens 159

(Qingdao Communication) The construction of the National Shandong University Science Museum started on March 5, 21st year, and was completed on January 10th this year. Because of the internal equipment, the purchased materials arrived late, and it was only completed in mid-March. A grand opening ceremony was held at 9:00 am on April 1st. Those who attended the ceremony at that time included Mayor Shen Honglie, the representative of the Ministry of Education, Dr. Bing Nongshan, Director of the Biological Research Institute of the Chinese Science Society in Nanjing, Zhang Jinmou, Dean of the Faculty of Arts and Sciences of Zhejiang University, Lei Fazhang, Director of the Education Bureau, Jiao Lu Commissioners Long Mengxiong, Liang Shijie, Chen Yanwen, and representatives from all walks of life, about 400 people. After the meeting was held as scheduled, Zhao Qi, President of Shandong University, reported on the process of establishing the museum. Then Shen Honglie, Bing Nongshan, Zhang Jinmou, Cui Shijie, etc. gave speeches successively. Then Mayor Shen performed the opening ceremony. All the guests freely entered the museum for visits. Each room was staffed with receptionists to guide and explain. The internal equipment was complete, and everything was available. The museum is a three-story building. The first floor is the Physics Department, which includes the Heat and Physical Properties Laboratory, the Ordinary Physics Laboratory, the Modern Physics Laboratory, the Wireless Electricity Laboratory, the Magnetoelectricity Laboratory, the Physics Storage Room, the Physics Classroom, the Metalworking Room, the Instrument Room, the Research Room, and the Auditorium. The second floor is the Biology Department, which includes the Botany Laboratory, the Biology Laboratory, the Histology Research Room, the Animal Physiology Research Room, the Plant Physiology Research Room, the Breeding Room, the Sectioning Room, the Plant Specimen Room, the Embryology Research Room, the Invertebrate Zoology and Oceanography Laboratory, the Vertebrate Zoology and Anthropology Laboratory, the Darkroom, etc. The third floor is the Chemistry Department, which includes the Quantitative Analysis Chemistry Laboratory, the Qualitative Analysis Chemistry Laboratory, the Physical Chemistry Laboratory, the Organic Chemistry Laboratory, the Sulfide Room, the Drug Room, the Balance Room, the Dispensing Room, the Instrument Room, the Library, the Specimen Room, the Pharmaceutical Chemistry Laboratory, the Combustion Room, the Research Room, the Darkroom, etc.

The Ministry of Education orders the adoption and promotion of phonetic symbols 160

(Nanjing, 4th) The Ministry of Education, according to the National Mandarin Education Promotion Association, presented four measures for promoting phonetic symbols, which were considered feasible and have been ordered to be adopted by various bureaus and halls.

Local News

The Ministry of Education commends Ye Hongying for donating huge assets 161

Enthusiastic public welfare is commendable

丨Family members express concerns about living expenses

Ye Hongying, a giant businessman, generously donated more than one million yuan of private property to run libraries and rural education, and invited Cai Zimin and other fifteen people as directors. The Hongying Education Foundation Board of Directors will be established soon. The origin and Chapter 1 of the rules have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a continuation of the recorded rules, postscripts, and documents submitted to the Ministry of Education and the Ministry's approved original text.

Chapter 2: Business. Article 4: Scope of the business purpose of this legal person, namely, to establish libraries in Shanghai City, and to establish rural primary schools in the vicinity of Shanghai and adjacent areas, from near to far. The construction costs of each school shall be determined by the donor. After the donor's death, it shall be decided by the following board of directors meeting. The subsidiary funds of each item of property in Chapter 1 of these rules shall be used for the operating expenses of the library and rural primary schools. The expenses of these two businesses shall not exceed half of the subsidiary funds. When there is a surplus of annual subsidiary funds, it shall be incorporated into the foundation. Article 5: Name. The name of this legal person is "Hongying Education Foundation," and the business it operates is "Hongying Library" or Hongying Rural First (or Second or ······) Primary School. Chapter 3: Organization. Article 6: Number of directors and their production. This legal person shall have fifteen directors to form a board of directors, which shall be filled by the donor and the personnel selected by him. After the donor's death, one person shall be selected from his descendants to supplement it, and his powers shall be the same as those of ordinary directors. Except for those designated by the donor during his lifetime, their production and removal shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 10 of this chapter. Article 7: Term of office of directors. The term of office of directors is for life. Article 8: Standing directors. The directors may mutually elect three to five standing directors. Article 9: Staff. The directors may hire staff. Article 10: Supplement and resignation of directors. If a director resigns, he may be dismissed with the consent of more than three-quarters of the directors. Article 11: Custody Committee. All the property of this legal person shall be designated by three people in the board of directors to form a custody committee during the donor's lifetime, and shall be jointly managed by the donor, but all the directors may supervise it. After the donor's death, the board of directors shall organize a custody committee to manage it and be supervised by all the directors. Chapter 4: Guarantee. Article 12: Convention. This legal person shall never change the scope of business stipulated in Article 4 and the name stipulated in Article 5. Article 13: Registration. This legal person and its rules shall be registered with the competent government agency for record. Chapter 5: Supplementary Provisions. Article 14: Handling of matters not covered. Matters not covered in these rules shall be handled in accordance with the general rules of legal persons of foundations. (C) Postscripts. (1) In addition to the various properties listed in Chapter 1 of these rules that have been donated to this legal person and the property at No. 6164 English Book, Xiafei Road, Shanghai French Concession, Hongying also plans to gradually donate the meager profits after the end of a small number of businesses to this legal person, and everything shall be handled in accordance with these rules. In addition, there are no other properties. As for the properties that have been given to each child and grandchild, they have been distributed and received, and they shall also be regarded as the property of non-donors and shall not be regarded as inheritance, unless otherwise specified in a separate will. This statement is attached. (2) Support. If the situation changes and the donor's life is difficult, all the property of this legal person shall be responsible for providing support for the donor's reasonable living expenses. (3) Wishes. The donor has this aspiration, but it is just to do his best. If Chinese people jointly continue to organize similar social undertakings, or assist the development of this legal person with funds, that is what he wishes. Ye Hongying, March 6, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

Document submitted to the Ministry of Education: Document submitted to the Ministry of Education to report the establishment of the Hongying Education Foundation Legal Person by. It is hereby requested to approve the establishment of the Legal Person by Hongying, who intends to use the funds for old-age care and the property enjoyed under his name, in accordance with the provisions of the attached rules, to fully fund education and cultural undertakings and establish the Hongying Education Foundation. In addition to the detailed explanation of the origin rules and property catalog of the donation in the attached rules, it should be prepared in accordance with the provisions of Article 59 of the General Principles of the Civil Law to request the Department to approve the permission. This is really a kindness. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Education, Person submitting the document: Ye Hongying.

Approval order from the Ministry of Education: The Ministry of Education's approval letter No. 1996, originally submitted by Ye Hongying, one document, requesting the establishment of the Hongying Education Foundation, approved the opening of the document, and all the documents were known. The document presenter generously donated private property to run education and cultural undertakings, and his enthusiasm for public welfare is commendable. The request to establish the Hongying Education Foundation shall be approved. The document is stored. This is the approval. Zhu Jiahua, March 9, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

Statement from family members: Ye's move is commendable, but according to his family members, it is said that Ye Jun had no choice but to do this due to family debts and litigation, regardless of the economic situation of his children and grandchildren. The family members did not know about this move beforehand. Therefore, when he invited his friends to discuss the method on the afternoon of the 3rd, two of his children and grandchildren requested to attend the meeting and made a public statement, stating that they had huge debts due to the influence of the current situation. If all the property is used for social undertakings, they are afraid that their children and grandchildren will have nothing to live on. Please understand their difficulties and take into account both social undertakings and livelihood issues, and ask for fairness and compassion. It was once believed by the gentlemen present that there was still value in considering the matter and that the board of directors would have a fair solution when it was formally established.

Second Session of the Inter-School Games Registration Deadline Set 168

From April 10th to 20th

Group Standard and Sports School Participation Methods Determined

No Individual Championship, Separate Awards for Overall Team Victory

The Sports Section of the Health Education Committee of the Municipal Education Bureau held its fifth meeting yesterday. Committee members present included Director Pan (represented by Ma Chonggan), Zhou Feicheng, Chen Bai, Ma Chonggan, Wang Keyong, Li Wanyu, Lu Bingqian, and Shen Siliang, with inspector Shao Rugan attending as an observer. Lu Bingqian chaired the meeting. The meeting approved the competition guidelines for this year's Inter-School Joint Sports Meet and the methods for sports schools to participate in the competition. It was also decided that registration for participation in the competition by each school should be from April 10th to 20th. Late registrations will not be accepted. The grouping standards for track and field events are as follows: for boys, those weighing 115 pounds or more and/or being 63 inches or taller will be considered Group A; those weighing less than 115 pounds and shorter than 63 inches will be Group B. For girls, those weighing 100 pounds or more will be Group A; those weighing less than 100 pounds will be Group B. Sports schools will participate in the same sports as ordinary middle schools. However, each athlete is limited to a maximum of four track and field events for boys and three for girls. Each school can send a maximum of four athletes per group per event. There will be no individual championships for men's and women's track and field events. Separate prizes will be awarded to the team with the highest overall score. The section also decided that with the sports meet approaching, all preparations must be made, and a sixth meeting will be convened next Monday (April 10th) at 2:00 PM at the Education Bureau.

Gongtie (Industry and Railway) Exhibition Football Performance: Donghua Wins Over Jiaotong University 171

Result: 3-2

Yesterday, at the Jiaotong University Industry and Railway Exhibition football performance, Donghua played against Jiaotong University at the large sports field starting at 2:30 PM. Many fans came to watch. Both sides had talented players, and the performance was excellent. As a result, Donghua won 3-2. The referee was Zhou Jiaqi. The lineups for both sides were as follows:

Donghua:

Chen Jinjiang (subbed out)

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Guan Xun'an, Tu Kaiyuan, Feng Yunyou, Feng Nianhan, Yang Renwei, Cao Qiuting, Li Yichen, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Yutian

Jiaotong University:

Fan Jiaju, Zhang Ji, Zeng Wangchang, Wu Youliang, Yang Xinghua, Zhang Jinrong, Wan Xianghua, Zhou Guangzhong, Liu Ximeng, Wen Liandong, Li Chuanxin

The first half started with a score of 1-0. Jiaotong University kicked off against the wind, and their attack was not smooth. Donghua repeatedly entered Jiaotong University's territory, but to no avail. Both sides attacked and defended, and the stalemate lasted for about half an hour. Both sides experienced dangerous moments, but neither side scored. Later, Donghua's Cao Qiuting resisted the enemy bravely and broke through two barriers in a row. He passed the ball to Chen Jiaqiu, who scored a goal. Jiaotong University's Wan Xianghua launched several attacks from the flanks and delivered wonderful passes, but there was a lack of players in the center to respond, and no one to shoot at the goal, resulting in many missed opportunities.

In the second half, the score was 2-2, and the teams switched sides to continue the battle. After five minutes, Li Yichen, with the help of Tu Kaiyuan, scored a goal without much effort. As a result, the forward momentum of their attack became stronger, and Jiaqiu and Yutian coordinated well. Li Yichen, with their help, scored the third goal. Jiaotong University suffered this setback and launched a vigorous counterattack. Sure enough, after only two minutes, Liu Ximeng scored a goal. Finally, Wen Liandong, with the help of Li Chuanxin, also scored a goal. As a result, Donghua won 3-2.

Soochow University Basketball Team Returns to Shanghai from Nanjing 174

First Game: Soochow University Wins Over Military Academy 35-33

Second Game: Soochow University Suffers a Close Loss 29-34

| Game Against St. Thomas University on the 9th |

The Soochow University basketball team, with its outstanding talent and profound skills, took advantage of the spring break and, led by Lu Zhongen, traveled with team members Feng Nianhua, Qian Jingyong, Wu Guolin, Lu Zhongen, Sun Baoqing, and others to Nanjing to compete against the Central Military Academy basketball team. Soochow University first won 35-33, then lost 29-34. The team returned to Shanghai by night train from Nanjing yesterday morning. It was learned that the team departed from Shanghai by night train on the 30th and arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 31st, staying at the Military Academy. Because they had not slept all night, the players were in poor spirits. The team requested that the game that evening be changed to the 1st, but the Military Academy stated that the tickets for the game had already been reserved and it was inconvenient to postpone it. Soochow University had no choice but to rest briefly and competed that evening at the Central University gymnasium. However, the basketball used was crooked and not round, and it was excessively heavy and unsuitable for use. Soochow University requested that the standard ball borrowed from the National Sports Association be used, but the Military Academy refused. As a result, each side used their own ball for half the game. Soochow University was at a disadvantage in the first half using the Military Academy's ball, but reversed the defeat and won in the second half using the Sports Association's ball. The second game was held on the evening of the 3rd. The Military Academy refused to use the Sports Association's ball again, and Soochow University requested that a standard ball be purchased for use, but the Military Academy said that it was impossible to purchase one. Soochow University had no choice but to continue using the Military Academy's ball, and as a result, they lost. As for the selection of the direction of the basketball hoops during the game, the drawing method was still used, and there was no distinction between host and guest. It is also heard that Soochow University has decided to play against the Philippine basketball champion St. Thomas University team on the 9th.

Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn)

Jews 179

— Hua Ling

| | Those Who Lost Their Nation Are Better | |

I never thought that the Jews, who have been without a country for so long, would still be feared and excluded in 1933, something even my family's Mr. Liu Renwen never dreamed of.

The Jews' ability to amass wealth and do business is many times greater than that of our country's respectable merchants who specialize in selling inferior goods. Taking Shanghai as an example, the great tycoon Hardoon cannot be compared with the big entrepreneurs who auction off their estates after their deaths.

The Jews have not only produced Hardoon in China, but in Europe, there are countless Jews who are richer than Hardoon and control the European economy. In the Americas, there is also the top-notch oil tycoon Rockefeller, who is also a Jew.

The Jews not only occupy an important position in the world's economy, but also contribute significantly to academia and science. The famous Mr. Einstein, who specializes in relativity, is one of the well-known Jews.

Speaking of Jews, they have a great background. There is also Comrade Marx, who is famous all over the world and will be remembered for thousands of years. When thieves see him, they laugh; when rich people see him, they jump. This old fellow brutally scooped out the core of history from "politics" and put it into the cavity of "economics", causing the unrestrained thoughts of today's youth and the terrifying situations everywhere.

The destruction of the Jewish state was inevitable, but it has produced so many great men, which shows that the destruction of a state is not a problem. After Jesus, so many famous people came out. After Confucius and Mencius, once our country is destroyed, after a thousand or eight hundred years, there will surely be some heroes who will shock the world and make the ghosts cry.

German Jews are being abused and excluded by Germans, and the stateless Jews scattered in various countries are united in boycotting Germany. Chinese people in foreign countries who have not lost their country are abused and excluded by the governments of their countries of residence, and the overseas Chinese elsewhere mostly eat more and say less. It is said that only slaves of a fallen nation need to unite. If we lose our country for a long time, we will surely learn that trick from the Jews.

New Era Yuefu (Ballads) 180

— Hu Jingping

Fight? Fine! I can't stand this insult at all! You want to attack Peiping? It's probably still early. Let's move the antiques to Nanjing first, and the students must run to Xi'an. Fine, you can come now, bombard with cannons, sweep with machine guns. What a joke, let's see if you can take away this place, or gnaw it down!

Tsk! Right! We have made this great determination, we are sure to scare the Japanese devils away! Now we are prepared for a long-term resistance, if you want to fight, you must also prepare a large sum of uncounted military expenses. Your equipment is good, but you suffer a loss, we only resist with spirit, do not fire cannons or guns, do you know how expensive a bullet is? Doing stupid things, we Chinese will not do. Moreover, we must be both loyal and filial, how can we let you injure our bodies and hair for nothing? Besides, have you learned any manners? Do you understand shame?

Fine! Fight! If you shamelessly occupy Peiping, we will move the antiques and students to Luoyang again. If you bombard Nanjing, and come to Luoyang to make trouble, we will unceremoniously run into Sichuan. There, all are dangerous waters, all are high mountains. Come? Are you afraid of the tigers in the mountains and the rapids in the water? If you still want to come, then... then... why bother, just don't give us any face? The place is occupied by you, the prestige is shown by you, and our long-term resistance and spiritual resistance are also cancelled, friend, what will make you happy? The days are long, the scientists have not yet calculated when the earth will be destroyed, you and I should keep some friendship, so we can meet again in the future.

Record of Jiaotong University's Industry and Railway Exhibition 181

— Cheng Zhizheng

The Industry and Railway Exhibition of Jiaotong University opened last week. Having been away from my alma mater for almost two years, I was naturally excited to take part in this grand commemorative opportunity.

After two years of separation, my alma mater seems to be different in everything. We followed the arrow signs and moved forward. The first thing we saw was the road city exhibition. Inside were construction reports of municipal roads in various provinces, especially the municipal design model of Hankou was the most exquisite. The gymnasium was an exhibition of student achievements. The industrial exhibition was in the industrial building, divided into two floors, with as many as thousands of kinds of exhibits. Various machines and electrical appliances could also be tested on the spot. Automatic telephones could be used for on-site calls, and the Great Northern Telegraph Machine could receive and send messages on behalf of customers. Once the words were written at one end, the telegram was immediately received at the other end.

Large machines were displayed in the shed, and some were in operation. A relatively new and curious exhibit was the Jiangfeng aircraft of the Navy. The upper courtyard was the railway exhibition. Various railway bureaus had exhibits on display, especially the model of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, which was exquisite and lovely, and the most unique. From Nanjing to Ningbo, the tracks were winding, there were also platforms and signals, a small bag of rice was placed in the rice-producing area, a pile of coal was placed in the coal-producing area, and bright electric lights were hung on the electric poles along the line, and the train was running from time to time.

Around the school, a small railway was laid by Jardine Matheson, with a circumference of about half a kilometer. A diesel engine pulled four or five passenger cars, which ran at any time. Curious ladies rushed to be the first to take a ride. In this Industry and Railway Exhibition, there is one more thing worth noting, and that is the completion of Rong Hong Hall. Since Li Yaosheng became the principal, Jiaotong University's atmosphere has suddenly become vigorous. Zhixin West Zhai, Ferguson Sports Ground, Industrial Building, and Rong Hong Hall General Office have all been completed in a very short period of time. Here, we have to admire the greatness of the construction power, and express our admiration to Principal Li, who has worked hard and made great achievements.

A Half Day in Longhua 182

— Fu Jingjia

The spring is gradually getting stronger. In order not to let it down, Hua and I decided to go to Longhua to inquire about the news of the peach blossoms. We rented two bicycles and enthusiastically set off for Longhua.

Gradually, we entered the embrace of the countryside. The fields were all green, and the willows along the road released yellow-green buds. Hua was extremely happy and sang a happy spring.

Longhua Pagoda was seen, how tall and majestic. The environment of the countryside is enviable enough. Hua said, "I must live in the countryside in the future."

What was unsatisfactory was that the peach blossoms had not yet bloomed. But we already felt that the spring was indeed strong.

In the setting sun, in the sound of returning sparrows, we returned to this dusty city again.

Random Notes on a Rainy Street 183

— Mingyuan

The rain kept falling, drizzling, drizzling. The entire street was shrouded in gloom and dimness. The signboards of the big stores standing out in the center of the street were lonely and drifting in the breeze and drizzle. Those square signboards with words like "official sauce" and "southern ham" were all crying and about to shed tears.

"Tell the news and sing the news! Da...da..." While singing, Douer beat the clapper. The vagrant's singing trembled through the empty street. He had a head of disheveled long hair; the breeze lifted the front of his gray-brown single cloth gown, revealing two thin yellow legs without socks; the mud splashed from the bottom of those broken shoes with holes in the front and back naturally glued the back of the gown to the calf.

The wandering monk held one hand in front of his chest and kept beating the big wooden fish hanging in front of him with the other hand; his lips moved, and after walking a distance, he knelt piously on the muddy road! He kowtowed piously...

"Aiya ai! Beng tong beng!..." Over there came the drum players! Look at the pair of men and women, with their heads wrapped in a square cloth and tied with waistbands and leggings, they may be from Fengyang... They sang along from house to house... "Do a good deed!..." A beggar dragged a wooden-wheeled cart with the upper half of another beggar's body on it, the lower half was an unattached infant leg that could rotate; and another bloody and festering leg stump...

The number of pedestrians was strangely scarce!

The arms of the rickshaw pullers hung despondently from the empty rickshaw handles.

The entire street was shrouded in gloom and dimness 丨 The rain was still falling, drizzling! Drizzling...

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 184

Small Knowledge

Common Knowledge of Treating Illnesses with Fruit 185

— Chu Yu

(Watermelon) We should pluck and cut the stems of watermelons in the early morning, before the sun rises, without using knives, scissors, or similar tools (avoiding copper or iron), and instead use stones to break the stems. This watermelon has absorbed dew and hasn't been exposed to sunlight, so its sweetness and moisture are very abundant, which has the effect of clarifying the blood. Elderly people who eat it can treat kidney diseases, strokes, jaundice, beriberi, and disorders of the urethra, bladder, and heart. Eating a little before or after ordinary meals can gradually alleviate various diseases. If you have a cold with a high fever, eating a little watermelon can prevent kidney inflammation. Nowadays, Western medicine uses watermelon sugar to make medicine for kidney diseases and watermelon puree to make medicine for acute enteritis, catarrhal dysentery, and other diseases. Eating it when returning home tired on hot days can eliminate fatigue. Eating a few pieces of watermelon before labor or when planning to climb a mountain can increase strength. People who like meat can neutralize the irritation of meat. However, eating too much watermelon after 4 PM can cause abdominal cold and inevitable problems. Therefore, young children must pay attention. If bitten by bedbugs, wiping the bite with watermelon juice can treat the marks. My family has a wonderful formula for dysentery, which I now make public for readers: use very ripe, large watermelons, remove the seeds, chop them up with the rind, squeeze the juice in a cloth bag, put it in an earthenware pot, and simmer it over a low heat. When it's reduced by half, add four taels of rock sugar, stirring constantly for about five minutes, then seal it in a bottle. Anyone suffering from dysentery can drink one spoonful on an empty stomach every day, and it will surely be cured.

(Pear) Generally, when patients have a high fever and no appetite, chewing pears and swallowing the juice has a remarkable effect in relieving fever. Nowadays, many cooling agents in Western medicine are made with pear juice. If elderly people peel, chop, and boil pears with a little salt, it can relax muscles and promote blood circulation. If you remove the core, add rock sugar, steam until cooked, and squeeze the juice with a cloth, it can stop coughs.

(Fig) is a good medicine for treating hemorrhoids. Eating the fruit and using the leaves to make a decoction is even more effective. If you eat it every morning, it can not only moisten the intestines and relieve constipation, but also treat dysentery. In winter, if you pick a catty of figs, first wash them with salt water to remove any moisture, peel them, add four taels of rock sugar, and one cup of clear water, boil for twenty minutes to make a syrup. People with hemorrhoids can spread it on bread and eat it every morning, or use half a spoonful of vinegar and one spoonful of fig syrup, mix with boiling water, and drink it.

(Grape) Grapes have the richest nutrients among fruits. Foreign countries use eating grapes as an effective medicine for treating brain diseases and neurasthenia. However, when using this fruit for medicinal purposes, the seeds should not be removed, and eating more grapes is also harmless. If we take red and black small-grained grapes, cook them (without adding water), and store the grape juice in a bottle, we can mix it with boiling water and a little white sugar during winter colds and flu, and the effect will be remarkable. Drinking a little grape juice every night can prevent colds.

(Peach) When peaches are used as medicine, they have astringent properties, but unripe or spoiled peaches should not be eaten, as they can cause stomach and intestinal problems. There used to be a saying: eating peaches in the dark is very beneficial. In general, eating more peaches is very effective for skin injuries, sores, and other diseases.

We should understand the effects of the above five fruits on the human body, but no matter what it is, it should not be eaten excessively. It is best to eat it at the appropriate time and with the appropriate amount.

Correction: In the Shanghai Night Talk article "Smoking Shops," there are many misprinted characters, which are corrected as follows: (1) "French for Tobaco" should be changed to "French for Tabac" (2) "Spanish for Tabago" should be changed to "Spanish for Tobaco" (3) "Tabasco, one of the British islands" should be changed to "Tabago, one of the British islands" (4) "Tobacco in the Gulf of Mexico" should be changed to "Tabasco in the Gulf of Mexico" (5) "Xibagu" should be changed to "Danbaku."

Free Talk

On the Topic of Commodities 186

— Da Wu

As soon as the national crisis arrives, telegrams are sent, volunteers enlist, officials sit tight, and donations are collected. It seems that everyone is of one mind, "sharing the national crisis together." However, "a brave soldier risks his life on the battlefield, while beauties dance in the general's tent." Some are "fighting hand-to-hand" on the front lines, while others are laughing and dancing with women in the rear. The other day, I was dragged to the Ambarsador by two friends, and I was shocked to see so many people dancing during this "national crisis." This is not to say that everyone has to be crying during a national crisis. There is no explicit legal provision against it, and although I "dare not lag behind others in loving my country," I have no deep resentment towards those who "do not forget entertainment while saving the country, and do not forget saving the country while entertaining." However, when I think of some people fighting bloody battles, while others, even if they contribute a little to "saving the country through aviation" or "saving the country through dancing," are still indulging in revelry, doing nothing, at least it cannot help but make people feel a sense of inequality among humans...

But what I want to say now is not about this.

"Like entering a shop full of abalone, you won't smell its stench after a long time." Friends who are always flipping and somersaulting in the human flesh market will not feel the ugliness of this market, but those who enter this foreign civilized dance floor for the first time cannot help but wonder what this society is really built on. Everything here has become a commodity: a woman's body is a commodity, and a woman's smile is also a commodity. Sinclair said that in the slaughterhouse, everything is useful except for the pigs' cries. I dare say that in this dance floor, even human breathing is a commodity (naturally, of women!). But this situation is not limited to the dance floor. I remember once going to a large hotel to meet a friend. I sat for two hours and saw a girl come in three times, each time dropping a flyer for female physiognomists. The text on each flyer was the same except for the name of Miss XX and the different photos, which proved that these were three different ladies. The flyer uniformly stated: "In addition to discussing physiognomy, all entertainment is declined," "Unwarranted gifts are respectfully declined," "Protecting personality and reputation is XX's only purpose," "Gentlemen, if you do not wish to discuss physiognomy, please do not invite." ...... If discussing physiognomy is a legitimate profession, why declare this? If you have to declare it, it shows that this profession has at least been exploited, and now it has been exposed. My friend said that this statement is precisely to tell you that you can inquire. It can be seen that there is another commodity here waiting for a price.

Someone else returned from Europe and passed through Saigon, where they saw that the opium dens there were posting advertisements for "new female attendants." So the commercialization of women has reached everywhere, universally.

Now that everything in China is being used to save the country, it seems inevitable that the above-mentioned commodities will also be borrowed to save the country.

Elementary School Teacher (Continued) 187

— Written by H. Barbusse, Translated by Li Qingya

丨丨 Please don't speak! said the elementary school teacher, at this moment his face was ashen, his eyes staring straight ahead, his hands trembling slightly.

But the donkey-like roar of his opponent was even more pleasant to hear:

丨丨 You are lying! You are lecturing lies as homework. You are insulting this religion...... Justice...... Humph, justice! One should not talk about justice to Christians, it has nothing to do with Christians, justice is God. What should be talked about to Christians is only faith and love.

In front of the terrified students in the classroom, he shouted the word love at their teacher with an angry and forceful attitude, so this one had to retreat a few steps, his face even more ashen than before, and his eyes also widened. Then the students all stood up, causing a disturbance. He felt that he had failed and stammered:

丨丨 You are a rogue.

He had just vaguely said the last few words when the deputy priest pounced on him and grabbed his arms, and the head priest raised his hand to prepare to strike.

But the deputy priest didn't grab his arms tightly, because at that time there were two gunshots. The head priest fell to the ground, motionless like a pile of things, and the deputy priest struggled after falling but couldn't hold on.

Finally, this fierce elementary school teacher woke up from his own fanaticism, and then fired a third shot, and fell beside the two.

This is the situation in 1926, in a large country, where an elementary school teacher dared to talk to students about "justice" and died.

The record of this trivial matter was published by several bold daily newspapers, but it could not be found in the famous daily newspapers; everyone knows the purpose of the major newspapers, which is to conceal the truth.

Note: H. Barbusse was born in 1874. His early works include three types: a collection of poems, Weepers, and novels, Beggars and Earth. However, they did not attract much attention; it was not until 1916 that he published the book Fire, which described the lives of soldiers in the European War in a daily format, opposing the war of imperialism, and his reputation increased greatly, becoming a giant in the world of literature. Later, there were also two types of bright and serial novels, and three types of short story collections, such as We These People. At that time, the author founded Guangming Society in Paris, advocating human equality and opposing imperialism, and had moved from literary life to political movement, and also had many types of writings on society and history in the world. This article is published in Anecdotes (Faits Divers), e2, published around 1927 or 1928, with a total of twenty-five articles, divided into three volumes: (1) European War, (2) White Terror, (3) Others. This article is the first article in the third volume, which records the facts before Spain changed its Republican political system; as for the translation, it focuses on the meaning. Translator's note.

Evening Glow 188

— Luo Hong

We watched the blue sky reflected in the lake water.

The lake water was so clear and soft, gently rippled by the breeze, like delicate dimples of laughter. The blue sky was also wrinkled all over. I looked at Qian next to me, who was staring at the lake water in a daze, and said: "Qian, how do these many shallow dimples compare to those on the face of movie star Miss Hu?" Qian loves the dimples on people's faces the most.

"You're wrong. Qian isn't thinking about Miss Hu's dimples. She's thinking about that Mr. Lu. Look, these ripples are just like Mr. Lu's bright eyes."

When Ping said this, I laughed. I thought of Mr. Lu coming to see Qian at our residence in the morning. Qian didn't say anything to deny it, just put on a coy smile and talked to friends on another boat. There were eight of us in this group, sitting on two boats, and we were sailing side by side.

The blurry distant mountains half embraced West Lake. Some buildings were reflected in the lake water, showing many black shadows, wriggling there. I had a strange yearning when I saw them. The boat slowly made another turn, and the place we had just passed became a golden strip of water. Many yachts were dragging such a golden strip, some slowly going away, and some lightly swinging over. The faces of the people on the boats were printed with light smiles, and their eyes had a dazed look, like sleepwalkers. Even more young men and women were sitting two by two on a boat, the breeze throwing their laughter into space, which was swallowed by the ripples on the lake.

"Let's go to Lakeside Park for a while." Someone on that boat suggested.

But we all opposed it, and didn't say anything. Only Qian said happily: "I like sitting on the boat like this the most. I can see everything. As long as there's a moon, I'd be happy to sit here all night tonight."

"Forget it. Mr. Lu is coming to see you tonight. You go play with him."

Everyone laughed. This group always likes to make jokes like that. The sun hung in the waist of the distant mountains, and the lake water shone even more like it was plated with gold. The scattered yachts all swung towards the side with the shining lights. On one side was the beautiful green mountain, and on the other side was the modern city market. The beautiful Xizi was wearing a modern dress. My companions began to sing popular songs. Only I was listening, looking at the lights reflected in the water, making my yearning dreams.

Random Words from Qu Lu 189

— Zi Zhan

(Thirteen) On Yi and Qi

When I first started writing, I liked to write profound and turbulent arguments. When I was young, after reading the Four Books, I secretly read Jin Shengtan's commentary on Romance of the Three Kingdoms. My tutor also ordered me to read Donglai Boyi, and Fan Gangjian. In Fan Gangjian, I liked Hu Zhitang's commentary the most. This man had a deep sense of morality and was particularly eager to defend the Tao. All historical figures who were not in the orthodox line of Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, Duke of Zhou, and Confucius were deeply criticized and overthrown. In Romance of the Three Kingdoms, I was addicted to reading Jin Shengtan's comments before each chapter, thinking they were profound and clever, almost memorizing every paragraph. As for Donglai Boyi, I only liked its overturning of cases. I was deeply influenced by Jin Shengtan, Hu Zhitang, and Lu Donglai, but I didn't know it at first. My tutor, Mr. Mou, taught the Records of the Grand Historian, and gave the topic "On Yi and Qi". My essay roughly said that the Prince of Guzhu was fortunate to have a middle son, otherwise, Yi and Qi would have yielded the country and fled a hundred times, the throne would have been vacant, and would the country not have been destroyed and the sacrifice ended? This is being unfilial. If one knows that there is someone who can be established, but uses the yielding of the country as a noble act, using clever words to deceive the world, this is being unkind. If one is unbenevolent and unfilial, but people call them wise sages, isn't that slander? Mr. Mou wrote at the end of the essay:

The love of argument of petty people is like this? With the achievements of the two sons being so outstanding, they still cannot be spared, so what else can be said!

This uses Han Yu's words from the postscript to the biography of Zhang Zhongcheng, as Han Gong defended Zhang Xun and Xu Yuan from slander. After reading this comment, I admired Mr. Mou's intelligence, but I hated his meanness. At that time, Mr. Mou was posing as a hermit with purity and holiness, and his criticism of Yi and Qi was just what he envied. Not long after, Mr. Mou descended from Shouyang, and became a high-ranking official in the court.

Full-length Creative Work

The Crossroads of the Times and Love 190

— Zhang Ziping

"Where is your wife?"

Haiquan asked him after sitting down.

"The child is a little unwell. She went out to buy medicine...... Really, this is unreasonable! She's been gone for three or four hours, and she hasn't come back yet!"

The last sentence was probably scolding his wife.

"When did your wife go out?"

"She went out early in the morning."

"What time was it?"

"We don't have a clock, we have to ask the landlord downstairs to know. But the one downstairs isn't very accurate either. She probably went out around seven or eight o'clock."

Haiquan thought after hearing this that even if she went out at eight o'clock, it had been two or three hours. What exactly did she buy that took so much time?

"Lao Lin, can you go out and buy me two or three sesame cakes? I want them salty."

At this moment, a bitter smile appeared on Shiguang's face.

"You haven't had breakfast yet?"

"Who's going to make it for me! She got up early in the morning and went out. And the child keeps wanting to be held. As soon as I put him down, he starts crying badly...... Ah! I really don't want to live this kind of life anymore!"

After Shiguang said this, he sighed deeply. The child in his arms responded to his sigh with a loud cry.

"Ah! Ah!...... Ah!......"

Shiguang picked up the child and swayed him from side to side. The way he looked made people laugh, but his throat seemed to be stuck by something. The sound of "Ah, ah!......" was also sung very badly, not as clear and pleasant as his wife sang.

"Okay. I'll buy sesame cakes for you. Is three enough? You don't want fried dough sticks?"

"It's okay to buy two more fried dough sticks. There are copper coins in my drawer, you take them out."

"No. I have them here."

Haiquan said and ran downstairs. But as soon as he stepped out of the back door, he saw Cao Shiguang's wife walking into the alley with a small vegetable basket.

"Oh, Mr. Lin, when did you come? Why don't you sit for a moment? Are you leaving already?"

When she saw Haiquan, she seemed to have an indescribable joy, she was just saying and smiling. Haiquan saw that she looked a little better than yesterday. It was probably because she went out and put on makeup.

"No. I came out to buy sesame cakes for Lao Cao."

"Oh! Then I'm sorry, Mr. Lin. Don't buy them, Mr. Lin. I've already bought buns and came back......"

"Really?"

Looking at Qiuying's charming appearance, Haiquan unconsciously asked her the two words "Really?"

"Why would I lie about this!"

"Sorry."

He smiled and turned back into the alley. She came closer and walked all the way with her shoulder close to his. Haiquan smelled a strange

fragrance, it seemed to be the fragrant oil she put on her hair.

Remittance Banks Change Their Business 198

| Adding Several Special Transaction Items Starting Tomorrow |

Recently, remittance banks have been affected by the trend, making it difficult to extend credit. It is difficult to stick to old rules, so they are changing and creating new avenues. This year, many of these money shops have changed to imitate banking business. The first ones were Fu Yuan and Yin Tai, etc. Now, it is heard that Tong Qing Bank will also imitate them and has decided to add several special transaction items starting tomorrow (6th). All shops, factories, firms, and individuals can directly open accounts without introduction, and they are the same as existing transactions, with interest calculated once a month. The procedures seem to be more convenient than banks.

Investigation of Shanghai Warehouse Stock of Yellow Filature Yarn Due to Stagnant European Sales 211

Lu Filature Yarn: 3,800 bales / Sichuan-Hubei Filature Yarn: Slightly over 2,000 bales

The yellow filature yarn produced in Sichuan, Shandong, Hubei, and other provinces of China is widely sold to Europe and the United States. In recent years, due to the global economic panic, the sales of silk fabrics have been sluggish and prices have weakened. European and American silk weaving factories have strived to reduce costs, and Japanese silk has taken the opportunity to dump goods at low prices. Rayon has also surged in like a terrifying wave, causing the sales of Chinese silk in Europe and the United States to plummet. The purchasing power of Germany and Switzerland has declined. Yellow filature yarn from Sichuan, Shandong, and other provinces is difficult to sell due to high costs and low prices. Since the beginning of the year, financial turmoil overseas has repeatedly occurred, and the consumption of raw silk has greatly reduced. The sales of Chinese silk to Europe have become increasingly stagnant. The yellow filature yarn from Sichuan and Shandong is almost at a standstill. It is now found that the Shanghai warehouse stocks of the aforementioned yellow filature yarn total more than 5,700 bales, including 3,800 bales of Shandong yellow filature yarn and 1,967 bales of Sichuan-Hubei yellow filature yarn. The spring silkworms in various provinces are about to emerge. Before the spring cocoon market, there may be no possibility of dumping.

More than 600 pieces arrived on Jiang'an and other ships yesterday

Our Army Reinforces Counterattack on Shimen Village 215

Heavy Rain Last Night, No Fierce Fighting on the Front Lines

Enemy Aircraft Bombard Our Haiyang Town Rear Area in Large Numbers

(Beiping) After our army recovered Haiyang Town yesterday, it actively reinforced troops to the line of Shimen Village, Liujiang, and Haiyang Town. It is not easy to defend firmly unless all three places are obtained. The enemy is also aware of this intention, so it has increased 4,000 to 5,000 troops near that line. There was no major contact due to the heavy rain last night. There will be a major battle this morning. (5th Dispatch)

(Luanzhou) At 5:00 AM on the 5th, after Haiyang Town was recovered, 400 enemies repeatedly attacked fiercely, but were repelled. At 7:00 AM, enemy troops were very active seven miles northeast of Qinhuangdao, attempting to spy on Qin Island. Enemy aircraft heavily bombed Haiyang. Enemy aircraft reconnoitered in Funing, Lulong, and Qian'an. At noon, one aircraft came to Luan, circled once, and went east. (5th Dispatch)

(Beiping) On the morning of the 4th, Haiyang was once breached by the enemy, and the situation in Qin Island suddenly became tense. Thousands of refugees fled to the station, causing disorder. In the afternoon, we recovered Haiyang, and order was restored.

The Railway Bureau and Mining Bureau are finding ways to build straw sheds in the nearby forests to shelter the refugees from the rain, only accommodating the elderly, children, and women. The able-bodied men are still ordered to flee to the Luanjin area. (5th Dispatch)

(Beiping) A Tianjin telegram reports that our army captured Shimen Village last night. The reporter inquired with officials today, who said that they had not yet received a report. (5th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Starting yesterday, we dispatched a train of armored vehicles to protect the slow trains on the Beining Railway to and from Qin Island. (5th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The enemy recently stated that if our army counterattacks Gubeikou and Xifengkou, the enemy will occupy important locations on the Yuguan side. (5th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Most of the enemy troops in the Qinhuangdao Shimen Village area are advancing in separate routes today, making contact with our army in Qin Island, Beihekou, and other places. Our new defensive positions have been completely deployed. If the enemy invades, we will resolutely counterattack. (4th Dispatch)

(Beiping) This morning, more than a dozen enemy aircraft flew to Haiyang Town, Shenhebao, Qin Island, and other places to reconnoiter, and dropped bombs on the rear of our army in Haiyang Town. Our army suffered very little damage. (4th Dispatch)

Our Army Bravely Recaptures Haiyang 217

(Beiping) He Zhuguo telegraphed Ping on the 4th, stating that at 9:00 AM on the morning of the 3rd, about 3,000 to 4,000 enemy troops from the Japanese invaders' infantry, cavalry, and artillery attacked Haiyang Town along the Liuhe Railway. One part advanced from Anminzhai and Dawangzhuang to spy on Qin Island, and another part pressed on Pingshanying from Shangxiaping Mountain. Our army resisted bravely with all its strength. At 3:00 PM, three Japanese aircraft reconnoitered in Haiyang Town, and at the same time concentrated artillery fire and fiercely bombed the positions of our cavalry Wang Shi. Our officers and soldiers suffered heavy casualties. The stalemate lasted until dawn on the 4th, when the enemy increased its troops and launched a fierce attack on us, using aircraft and armored vehicles to assist in the battle, and attacked Haiyang Town. After a long and fierce battle with our army, the enemy once occupied Haiyang Town. Our front-line commander [illegible] commanded the [illegible] divisions and personally led the counterattack, fighting hand-to-hand for three hours. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Eventually, Haiyang Town was recaptured, and more than 2,000 remnant enemies retreated in disorder towards Taipingzhuang. We are currently pursuing them. (4th Dispatch)

Foreign Observers View the Situation in Qin Island 218

The British, due to mining and railway debt relations, will protest first. He Zhuguo is currently commanding near Beidaihe, and Qin's defense is secure. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Resolution of the Central Political Conference

Kong Xiangxi Appointed Governor of the Central Bank 223

Law on Changing Liang to Yuan Effective from April 6th

(Nanjing) The Central Political Conference held its 351st meeting on the morning of the 5th, attended by Yu Youren, Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Chen Guofu, Ye Chucang, Li Shizeng, Zhang Renjie, Wu Jingheng, Lin Sen, Zhang Ji, Shi Ying, Song Ziwen, Chen Gongbo, Zhu Jiahua, Zhou Qigang, and others, more than 30 people in total. Yu Youren presided over the meeting. The matters discussed were: (1) The drafting of the National Assembly Organization Law and Election Law bill was submitted to the Legislative Yuan's Constitution Drafting Committee to draft a principle draft and submit it to the meeting for approval. (2) The draft amendment to the Method of Appointing County Magistrates was submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review. (3) The organizational regulations of the Administrative Regulations Consolidation Committee were approved. (4) The Hunan Province National Salvation Donation case was submitted to the Finance, Military, and Legal Groups for expedited review. Before the review is completed, the party, government, and military organs in Hunan should be notified by telegram to stop the process. (5) The Minister of Finance, Song Ziwen, submitted a request to resign from his concurrent position as Governor of the Central Bank. It was resolved to approve the request and appoint Kong Xiangxi, a director of the bank, as the Governor. (6) It was resolved to establish a special court to punish customs corruption. (7) Regarding the change of Liang to Yuan, it was resolved that from April 6th of this year, silver dollars should be used for all public and private receipts and payments. Any calculations using taels of silver will not be legally effective. The export of currency materials will be taxed at a uniform rate of 2.25%. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Japanese Army Advances on Ningfeng 224
