The End of Airships?

Wireless Report from the Aftermath of a Catastrophe Describes the Tragic Loss of the US Navy Airship 233

Flying at an Altitude of 16,000 Feet in Gale-Force Winds and Rain

Terrifying Scene of the Sea Surface Illuminated by Electrical Discharges at Midnight

Seventy-Three People Including the Director of Naval Aviation Perished

Reuters, New York, 4th - Navy Major Wiley sent a wireless telegraph reporting the circumstances of the loss of the Navy airship Akron on the night of April 3rd from 10:00 PM to midnight. Wiley was one of three survivors, initially rescued by the German ship Phoebus and then transferred to the coastal patrol boat Cutter. The telegram was sent from the Cutter. This is the first official report received, stating that the Akron was surrounded by electrical discharges at 10:00 PM last night while flying at an altitude of 16,000 feet in gale-force winds and rain, constantly changing direction. It began to descend at midnight. Half an hour later, it dropped its ballast sandbags. At that time, there were still electrical discharges on all sides, and the turbulence was quite severe. During its descent, the stern was downwards. Suddenly, its rudder was lost, and the ship touched the surface of the water and was immediately destroyed. The sea was illuminated by incessant flashes of electrical discharge, creating a terrifying scene. At first, people were seen struggling to swim amidst the wreckage of the airship, but in an instant, they all disappeared. Before the destruction, the flight deck was completely calm, with no signs of panic, it is said.

Only Three Survivors Among Seventy-Six People in Distress 234

It has now been determined that there were 19 officers and 57 enlisted crew members on the Akron. The whereabouts of only five people are known. Four were rescued by the German ship Phoebus, but one died shortly after. The other, Navy Major McLelland, was recovered today. The three survivors are Navy Major Wiley, crew members Thiel and Owen. Navy Executive Officer Guffran, although rescued, later died on the Phoebus. The Navy patrol boat Cutter has today sent the three survivors ashore. They all refused to talk. Only Wiley, wearing a tightly fitting military uniform, mumbled that he was fine, it is said. Thiel was sent to the hospital on a stretcher after landing. He was also in distress during the loss of the US Navy airship Shenandoah in 1925. Several ships are still searching for the victims amidst the wreckage of the Akron floating on the sea surface, but they are facing great difficulty due to rain and fog. The location of the Akron's loss is about 20 miles from the Barnegat Lightship.

Two of a Total of Three Airships Have Now Been Lost 235

The loss of the Akron, according to general opinion, has dealt a fatal blow to airships. It is feared that no one will promote airships commercially or militarily from now on. Vincent, the chairman of the committee investigating the loss of the Akron, declared that no more airships would be built in the future. The United States built a total of three airships, and two have been lost. It is found that the United States spent US$20 million to build this type of airship, and the Shenandoah and now the Akron have been destroyed. Only one ship remains, named Macon. Navy Secretary Swanson said today that he has never been as enthusiastic about airships as others, and also said that the Akron's sister ship, Macon, will be sent to the West Coast to cooperate with the fleet as originally planned, it is said. One of the most prominent victims of the Akron was Rear Admiral Moffett, the Chief of the Bureau of Aeronautics. The National Aviation Monthly published an article by the admiral on the Akron in January 1932, stating that although the Akron was overweight, its navigation was not affected under normal conditions, and that the reason for the increase in weight was due to changes ordered by the Navy to improve its safety and military effectiveness, it is said.

The Airship Drifts Away with the Waves, the Hull is Completely Destroyed 236

Reuters, New York, 5th - Navy Major Wiley, wearing hospital clothes, told a group of reporters today about the circumstances of the loss of the Akron, stating that the airship showed no signs of being struck by lightning. There was no explosion or fire inside the ship. Near midnight, the airship began to descend rapidly. At that time, all engines were running at full speed. He threw all the ballast sandbags carried on the ship into the sea. The airship tilted forward to about 800 feet above the ground, then immediately rose. It stabilized at about 1,500 feet above the ground. Three minutes later, the air became unstable. The bow rose considerably. He knew he was near the center of a major storm, so he ordered everyone on board to prepare. The airship then tilted quite severely, and the control cables and the upper rudder were lost in the wind. Wiley then tried to steer with the lower rudder. He moved to the right side of the control machine to steer, while the captain was on the left side to operate the elevator. At that time, the bow was tilted upward at about 20 degrees. The ship dropped rapidly. Nothing could be seen outside the ship except for the heavy fog. He asked what the altitude was, and was told it was 300 feet. He then ordered everyone on board to prepare for the inevitable destruction. Everyone was calm and handled matters, but in an instant, the ship hit the water. Seawater poured in through the windows. He hurriedly swam out of the ship. When he reached the surface of the water, he saw the airship drifting away with the waves in the constant flashes of electrical discharge. The bow was facing the sky, and the hull was completely destroyed. Then he saw the lights of the Phoebus. He struggled to swim towards the ship, grabbing a board and swimming while holding it. He heard cries for help on the water. The Phoebus threw a rope into the water and hauled him onto the ship, but the others were farther away from the Phoebus.

Reuters, Atlantic City, 4th - Navy blimp No. 3, while searching for survivors at the scene of the Akron's loss tonight, crashed and sank in a gale. A seaplane flew to rescue them. It was initially reported that three of the eleven people on the blimp had drowned, but it was later learned that all were rescued.

Prelude to a British-Soviet Rupture 237

British Government Publishes Details of Negotiations

Reuters, London, 4th - The British authorities today published a White Paper disclosing documents from the British Ambassador to Russia, Voffan, reporting to the British Foreign Office after six British technicians from the Vickers Electrical Company were detained on March 12th. All six detainees, except for MacDonald, have been temporarily released, each on bail of 50,000 rubles. However, the Russian employees who were detained were not allowed to be bailed. British technician Monkhouse was interrogated for 19 hours. Monkhouse admitted that he regularly reported the business situation to Vickers Electrical Company based on reports from various technicians. The interrogator then pointed out that this was a criminal act of secretly inquiring for information. Monkhouse also admitted that 25% of Vickers Electrical Company's turbines were unsuitable for use, the reason being that the Russians did not want to use standard machines. Vickers Company is now quickly trying to correct various defects. British Ambassador Voffan wrote to the Foreign Office on March 14th, reporting on his visit to the prisons where British technicians Thornton and Gregory were detained, stating that "the two technicians had clearly endured hardship and were in unspeakable misery." On March 16th, the British Ambassador reported to the Foreign Office on his meeting with Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov. At that time, the British Ambassador stated that this was not a matter of sovereignty, but a question of whether the British could reside and conduct business in Russia. Litvinov replied that strong words would not have any effect on the Soviet government. At the end of the meeting, the British Ambassador stated that Russia was deliberately destroying British-Soviet relations and that he was very disappointed. He had initiated British-Soviet relations, and unfortunately, it seemed that he would be the one to sever them, it is said.

Reuters, London, 4th - The British government's bill submitted to the House of Commons to ban the import of Russian goods is quite concise, with only four clauses, advocating that the government should ban the import of all kinds of goods produced or manufactured by the Soviet Russian Federation by order. This bill will come into effect on April 18th. It does not apply to transit goods. The bill stipulates that any goods manufactured half in Russia and half elsewhere will be regarded as Russian goods unless it can be proved that the goods were completed elsewhere after leaving Russian territory, accounting for at least a quarter of their value. The bill also contains remedies for failure to fulfill contracts due to the declaration of the ban. The bill authorizes the Department of Trade to issue special licenses for the import of prohibited goods. After the second reading of the bill, opposition leader Cripps moved to strike down the bill this evening, stating that the White Paper did not show sufficient reasons why the British government required the unconditional release of the arrested persons, nor did it show sufficient reasons why the British government needed to obtain the special powers proposed in this bill for retaliatory reasons against Russia, it is said.

Reuters, London, 4th - A well-known London lawyer, Cazalet, who is fluent in Russian, will go to Moscow to defend the arrested British technicians in court if he is granted special permission by the Russian government.

Reuters, Moscow, 5th - Before being released on bail, the Russian authorities officially filed an indictment against British technicians Cushny, Thornton, and Gregory, accusing them of committing crimes of secretly inquiring for political and military information and damaging machinery. Thornton alone was also charged with bribery. The defendants all pleaded guilty. It is said that a Russian lawyer has agreed to defend the defendants.

TASS, Moscow, 4th - Three of the six British engineers from the detained Vickers Company, Keshina, Gregory, and Thornton, were released on bail today. However, all signed a statement not to leave Moscow and to appear in court when summoned. The bail money was paid by the company this morning.

Page 20

The League of Nations' Sanctions Against Japan 257

Japanese Foreign Ministry Study Concludes They Cannot Be Implemented

(Special Dispatch from the Japan League News Agency) The Japanese government has now withdrawn from the League of Nations. However, before making that decision, the Japanese Foreign Ministry studied the various issues that would arise after withdrawing from the League, the impact on all aspects, and the feasibility of sanctions under Article 16 of the Covenant, to provide a basis for the fundamental principle of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations. As a result of this investigation, it was concluded that the sanctions under Article 16 could not be implemented. Thereupon, the Japanese government made the final decision and announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations on March 27. The Foreign Ministry's report to the government is very long. The following is a brief summary of the contents for the reference of the world.

Table of Contents of the Investigative Report 258

(I) The basic meaning of Article 16.

(II) Resolutions of the League of Nations that serve as guidelines for interpreting Article 16.

(III) Conditions for applying sanctions under Article 16.

A. Economic and military measures.

B. Expulsion.

(IV) Implementation of sanctions.

A. Overview

B. Severance of diplomatic relations.

(I) The relationship between the violating country and the League of Nations member states that declare war on it.

(II) The issue of whether it is an aggressive war.

(III) Sanctions against the aggressor country.

C. Economic blockade, the main point of Article 16.

(I) Economic blockade of the event itself; economic blockade under international law.

(II) The timing of the start of the economic blockade.

(III) Various measures of economic blockade.

(IV) Cooperation between countries and participation of non-member states in the economic blockade.

D. Military sanctions.

E. Expulsion.

(V) Expenses required for sanctions.

(VI) Article 16 and neutrality.

(VII) Difficulties in applying Article 16.

Interpretation and Application of Article Sixteen of the Covenant 259

(1) Having experienced the result of the World War, all nations deeply feel that the basic meaning and international obligation of Article 16 should be implemented and observed through international sanctions. Before the Great War, the implementation of international sanctions agreements barely existed in practice or regulations, so there were very few who firmly advocated this. In this sense, this article is the most important among the Covenant articles, and it attaches great characteristics to the organization of the League of Nations. Although there are many international associations, there are no other groups besides the League of Nations that stipulate common sanctions against countries that violate the association's charter. The application of this sanction is not limited to the violation of specific provisions of the Covenant (refer to Article 16, paragraph 1). It goes without saying that applying it to the violation of general regulations is in line with the spirit of the League of Nations.

(2) Resolutions of the League of Nations as a Guide to Interpreting Article 16: The League of Nations, in view of the imperfections of Article 16, the issue of its amendment or interpretation has long been a topic of discussion. The First League of Nations Assembly (1920) ordered the Council to establish an "International Committee on Blockade" to study the economic blockade issue in this article. The following year, the Second Assembly, after deliberation by various committees, adopted four draft amendments and a majority of interpretative resolutions. According to these proposals, they have not yet come into effect because they have not been sufficiently ratified (Article 26).

(3) Conditions for Applying Sanctions under Article 16:

A. Conditions for Economic and Military Measures (Article 16, Paragraph 1):

This sanction must be applied to "a member of the League of Nations that resorts to war in disregard of its covenants under Articles 10, 12, or 15." However, economic and military measures are not the only necessary sanctions in the above situations. Violations of Articles 10, 11, paragraph 1, 12, paragraph 4, 17, paragraph 4, etc., may also be considered. Then, who decides whether the act of violating these regulations constitutes the so-called "war of aggression"? According to the explicit text of Article 16 and paragraph 4 of the Second League of Nations Assembly resolution, it is a matter to be clarified by each country of the League of Nations itself with its legal authority. However, the following points should be noted regarding this matter:

(1) The independent right of each country to exist lies in Article 16, and there is absolutely no arbitrary exception. If a League of Nations country obtains confirmation of a violation of Article 16, it has the obligation to apply the sanctions of this article.

(2) A difficult situation will arise when the League of Nations countries cannot agree on the issue of whether a violation of the Covenant exists (for example, Country A declares war and imposes sanctions because it believes that Country B is carrying out a war of aggression, but another country believes that Country A has violated the Covenant). The Second Assembly hoped that the Council would issue an opinion on this issue by a majority vote and hoped that all countries would act according to this opinion. However, because the opinion is not binding, each country can still take independent action arbitrarily without waiting for the Council to issue an opinion. As a result, especially when a member country opposes the majority opinion of the Council and determines that a violation of the Covenant exists, an extremely dangerous situation will inevitably arise. The shortcoming of this article lies in this.

B. Expulsion (Conditions of Article 16, Paragraph 4): The sanction of expulsion is different from economic and military measures. It can be exercised when a country intentionally violates the Covenant.

(4) Implementation of Sanctions A. General Situation

Article 16 stipulates economic blockade, military sanctions, and expulsion sanctions as methods of sanctions. There is no problem with the expulsion section, but there is no definitive discussion on the extent of economic and military sanctions that each country should implement against violating countries. Also, in relation to this, the severance of diplomatic relations must be considered. The text of Article 16, paragraph 1, leads people to speculate and interpret that as a result of a war of aggression, a state of war is automatically established between the aggressor country and the entire League of Nations. According to this view, the entire League of Nations immediately expresses a war-like attitude toward the violating country, and at the same time, diplomatic relations are naturally severed, and preparations are made to implement severe economic and military systems when necessary. However, several countries of the League of Nations found this interpretation most painful, and the drafters of this text were also afraid that they could not obtain a reliable belief that it could be implemented. Therefore, the Second Assembly interpreted the explicit text of this article as "the unilateral actions of the violating country do not create a state of war, its actions only declare the implementation of war acts, or there is a possibility of a state of war between the violating country and the League of Nations countries. However, in the League of Nations, at least preventing war and attempting to restore peace through economic pressure is an act in line with the spirit of the Covenant (Resolution 2)." If there is a violation of the Covenant, it is not necessary to immediately realize all the effects of the economic blockade. Lighter measures can be implemented first, and then gradually more severe measures (Resolution 14). It goes without saying that when League of Nations countries recognize the existence of a war of aggression, they must implement economic sanctions (Article 16), but according to Resolution 3 of the previous paragraph, the right to declare war on the violating country rests with each country. Therefore, there are League of Nations member countries that do not want to participate in the economic blockade or declare war against the violating country (whether diplomatic relations are severed at this time will be described in the charter). The Second Assembly recognized the delegation of economic sanctions to two countries and allowed certain countries, under certain conditions, to postpone participating in all or part of the economic measures (Resolution 9 and the additional protocol of Article 18, paragraph 4). Therefore, with the permission of the Council, even if it is known that there is a violation of the Covenant, one can not participate in sanction behavior. That is, according to the resolutions and amendments of the Second Assembly, the obligations stipulated in this article can be slightly reduced. In other words, violating the explicit text of the Covenant is in line with the spirit of the League of Nations (but because this resolution is not binding, each country can also assert the opposite interpretation). However, granting the right to declare war immediately to the League of Nations countries can be said to be extremely dangerous. We still hope that all countries will postpone action until the Council issues its opinion.

B. Severance of Diplomatic Relations

(1) Diplomatic relations are naturally severed between the violating country and the League of Nations countries that declare war on it.

(2) League of Nations countries that do not declare war on the violating country also have the obligation to sever the following diplomatic relations to help ensure the absolute success of the economic blockade, but consular relations can continue (Resolution 12 of the Second Assembly).

(3) Sanctions against aggressor countries are carried out in the name of the League of Nations. Therefore, the League of Nations organs should also stop acting on behalf of the aggressor country, but the severance of diplomatic relations can be temporarily limited to recalling ambassadors or ministers (Resolution 11 of the Second Assembly). Also, people from violating countries who are staff members of the League of Nations Secretariat can remain in their original positions because they can be said to have renounced their nationality during their tenure.

C. The most important economic blockade among the sanctions stipulated in Article 16:

(1) The economic blockade in this article and the blockade under international law are different from the peacetime blockade or wartime blockade stipulated in traditional international laws and regulations.

That is, under traditional international law, there is no obligation under domestic law to prohibit this behavior. However, according to Article 16, it stipulates that each League of Nations country has a domestic legal obligation to prohibit its own citizens or merchant ships from communicating with the people of the violating country. Moreover, the League of Nations countries must prevent and suppress communication between the people of the violating country and other nationals. This kind of measure can be implemented on land or at sea, regardless of international laws and regulations. This is the difference from the so-called peacetime and wartime blockades. Therefore, there is no problem between League of Nations countries, but for non-League of Nations countries or League of Nations countries that do not recognize the continuation of the war of aggression and do not agree to apply the sanctions of Article 16, the blockade should be implemented based on general international law. Currently, peacetime blockades under international law cannot involve the ships of third countries, and for ships that violate blockade behavior, only the cargo can be detained, and the ship cannot be confiscated. Therefore, compared to wartime blockades, its effect is much less. Therefore, if the violating country has a maritime boundary, in order to achieve the complete purpose of the sanctions in this article, it is necessary to implement the economic blockade stipulated in this article and at the same time implement a wartime blockade. Also, the obligation stipulated in the latter part of Article 4, paragraph 1, to prevent and suppress financial, commercial, and personal communication between the violating country and all other countries cannot be exercised without implementing a wartime blockade. Therefore, even if the interpretation that the country that has taken the war of aggression and all other League of Nations countries are not in a state of war is established (refer to Chapter A above), the country participating in the economic blockade of the country with a maritime boundary must be in a state of war with that country.

(2) The time to start the economic blockade:

Article 16, paragraph 2 stipulates that all League of Nations countries should immediately sever all relations with the violating country. From the perspective of the original meaning of this item, each League of Nations country should start the economic blockade when it holds the firm view that there is a war of aggression, and should not wait for other countries to take this measure. However, for the success of the economic blockade, it is absolutely necessary for all countries to take unified action. Therefore, after the Council issues its opinion on the time, type, and degree of commencement of the economic blockade, each country can start action. The Second Assembly decided to revise this charter and stipulated that the Council should notify the League of Nations countries of the time for implementing economic sanctions (the third additional agreement), but the independent decision-making power of each country still exists.

Today's principle is that each country can start action at any time when it recognizes that there is a war of aggression.

(3) Measures taken by various countries regarding the economic blockade:

The latter part of Article 16, paragraph 1 stipulates that League of Nations countries should take measures to make the economic blockade effective against the violating country. According to this provision, any League of Nations country that recognizes a war of aggression must: (1) sever all commercial and financial relations between its own country and the violating country, (2) prohibit all communication between its own citizens and the citizens of the violating country, and (3) take active measures to prevent and suppress all commercial, financial, and personal relationships between other countries and the violating country.

The differences between rights and obligations and the rights and obligations of blockades under traditional international law have already been described. League of Nations countries must take domestic legislative measures to implement this obligation (Resolution 19 of the Second Assembly). Whether the above-mentioned (2) prohibition of communication should be implemented in the country of nationality or the country of residence is a major issue. The text of Article 16 seems to take the principle of nationality at first glance, but the Blockade Committee adopted the principle of residence, and the Second Assembly also adopted this claim (Resolution 13, the amendment to Article 16, paragraph 1). Therefore, residents of the blockading country and residents of the blockaded country shall not continue any relationship. However, imprisoning people from violating countries, detaining shops, and implementing actions should be prohibited. Later, the Fourth Congress decided to adopt the principle of residence as the principle, and League of Nations countries could arbitrarily use the principle of nationality at the same time, but these amendments have not come into effect. Therefore, it seems that League of Nations countries cannot be forced to implement the principle of residence under current law, but what should be most noted here is that the Second Assembly stipulated that each country does not have to immediately implement the most severe economic sanctions and can implement them in progressive steps (Resolution 14). Therefore, it is not necessary to immediately prevent all goods from being transported to the violating country, and it is possible to only prohibit the transportation of important items as a function of economic and military resistance.

(4) Cooperation between countries and the participation of non-member countries in economic blockade behavior:

When League of Nations countries implement Article 16, paragraph 3 regarding military and economic sanctions, they shall assist each other to avoid losses and keep them to a minimum. Regarding this kind of joint relationship between League of Nations countries, the Second Assembly requested that all countries accept the Council's advice, promise to undertake special tasks, and at the same time, for those countries that are severely affected by participating in joint sanction behavior, relax their participation or postpone it under certain conditions (Resolution 9 and the additional protocol of Article 4). The Council must strive to conclude agreements with non-League of Nations countries in order to cooperate (Resolution 17 of the Second Assembly), but it is impossible for the Council to conclude this kind of agreement with all non-League of Nations countries. Therefore, when implementing an economic blockade, it is also necessary to implement a wartime blockade at the same time.

D. Military Sanctions

The task of the League of Nations is to avoid declarations of war and military sanctions and restore peace through economic pressure (Resolution 3 of the Second Assembly). A declaration of war does not have to be combined with military measures. There are also declarations of war for demonstration purposes or to fully implement economic blockade behavior. For the application of military sanctions, the Council must propose to all League of Nations countries a system for the allocation of land, sea, and air forces by each country in accordance with Article 16, paragraph 2 to uphold the Covenant. This kind of proposal is also necessary in economic blockades and wartime (when wartime blockades are carried out at the same time). Each country shall participate in military sanctions to the extent necessary in principle, but the Council's proposal is not binding. Therefore, each country may refuse to participate in military sanctions with reasonable reasons, but this refusal does not deny the existence of legal restrictions. Although the League of Nations country that recognizes the war of aggression does not participate in military sanctions, it must allow the military of the country participating in military sanctions to pass through its territory, and it must also have the obligation to assist each other as stipulated in Article 16, paragraph 3. Therefore, this kind of League of Nations country does not have the rights and obligations of neutrality, but has a special position. All countries that oppose the violating country should act as organs of the League of Nations, and the League of Nations, in accordance with Article 11, considers the war between that League of Nations country and the violating country to be a matter of concern to the interests of the entire League of Nations and can intervene in this matter (according to the German international law scholar, Mr. Xijin).

E. Expulsion,

The expulsion sanction can only be implemented against the League of Nations country responsible for the war of aggression, but unless all the world's major countries participate in the League of Nations, the one who suffers the damage as a result of the expulsion is not the violating country but the League of Nations itself. The expulsion sanction cannot be implemented without the unanimous agreement of the Council (excluding the violating country).

(5) Expenses Required for Sanctions,

It is a matter of course that the violating country bears all the expenses required for its own actions and compensates for damages, but when various countries cannot fulfill this, the League of Nations bears the League of Nations' action expenses (especially military expenses), and each League of Nations country bears the losses suffered by each League of Nations country due to the economic blockade.

(6) Neutrality in Article 16

(1) Those who are completely neutral in the application of Article 16 are non-League of Nations countries that do not engage in wars of aggression and do not participate in sanctions.

(2) Although the League of Nations country does not declare war, it cannot be in a neutral position if it recognizes a war of aggression. It has a special measure, as described above. (3) What kind of position is a League of Nations country in that does not recognize a war of aggression and does not participate in the sanction behavior of Article 16? Whether these countries bear the obligations of Article 16, paragraph 3, is questionable. From the point of view of making the sanctions of the League of Nations easy to implement, if these countries bear their obligations, then their neutrality should also be restricted (according to Dr. Ritsuo Tateki). However, in the above sections (1 and 2), whether the violating country should willingly accept this neutral system is another matter. Also, when a non-League of Nations country refuses to accept the obligations of Article 17, paragraph 1 of the Covenant and wages war against a non-League of Nations country that accepts the opinions of the League of Nations (Article 17, paragraph 3), both countries are not bound by the Covenant as a result. All countries may demand that the League of Nations countries give up their neutrality, and the actions of the League of Nations countries in the above sections (1 and 2) violate neutrality.

(7) Conclusion (Difficulties in applying Article 16),

Although Article 16 is an important provision in the League of Nations Covenant, due to its specificity and the fact that the League of Nations does not have a worldwide nature, various difficulties arise when it is implemented. This can be roughly understood from the above-mentioned reasons. The application of this article has not been seen since the establishment of the League of Nations, because the one who suffers the damage is not the expelled country but the League of Nations itself. Although joint military sanctions seem powerful, it is impossible for the Council to decide on the number of land, sea, and air forces that each country should assume. Therefore, the initiation of sanctions under this article can be said to be absolutely impossible to realize. As for the most important economic blockade, it also seems difficult to implement for the following reasons:

(1) The economic and financial damage caused by the economic blockade to the violating country is quite large, but at the same time, the countries participating in the economic sanctions also suffer great losses and inconvenience, as mentioned above.

(2) The economic blockade must be accompanied by a wartime blockade, but the difficulty in implementing this military sanction has also been described (because non-League of Nations countries will not sacrifice their freedom and endure losses and inconvenience to assist in economic sanctions).

(3) There are various difficulties due to the incompleteness of the prescribed methods, as described above. Namely, (1) each country has independent decision-making power to determine whether or not to violate the treaty and implement economic sanctions, and it is feared that unified action cannot be taken, and the League of Nations may abuse the sanctions of this article with malicious intent. (2) The principle of nationality clearly stipulated in Article 16, paragraph 1, is actually quite difficult to implement (the revised regulations advocating the principle of residence have not yet become binding). (3) Various difficult problems arise due to neutral relations, and mutual assistance between League of Nations countries is not possible.

On-Site Representatives 266

(Chairman's Report) At precisely 10:00 AM, the meeting commenced as scheduled. Chairman Zheng reported that today marked the fifth drawing for redemption of the principal of the 20th Year of the Republic Short-Term Financial Public Bonds, the eleventh drawing for redemption of the principal of the 18th Year of the Republic Disbandment of Troops Bonds, and the second drawing for redemption of the principal of the 20th Year of the Republic Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bonds. He expressed his delight at the presence of the attendees. He then stated that the total issuance of the 20th Year of the Republic Short-Term Financial Public Bonds was 80 million yuan. With the first to fourth redemptions already drawn, this was the fifth redemption, with two lots to be drawn, each worth 80,000 yuan, totaling 160,000 yuan, which is two per thousand of the total issuance. Therefore, the lottery method would be to select bond tickets with the same last three digits. The total issuance of the 18th Year of the Republic Disbandment of Troops Public Bonds was 50 million yuan. With the first to tenth redemptions already drawn, this was the eleventh redemption, with one lot to be drawn, worth 500,000 yuan, which is one percent of the total issuance. Therefore, the lottery method would be to select bond tickets with the same last two digits. The actual issuance of the 20th Year of the Republic Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bonds was 6 million yuan. With the first redemption already drawn, this was the second redemption, with two lots to be drawn, worth 120,000 yuan, which is two percent of the total issuance. Therefore, the lottery method would be to select bond tickets with the same last two digits. For the three types of winning bond tickets, the 20th Year of the Republic Short-Term Financial Public Bonds and the 20th Year of the Republic Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bonds would be redeemed starting from the 15th of this month, and the 18th Year of the Republic Disbandment of Troops Public Bonds would be redeemed starting from the 30th of this month. Except for the Silk Industry Public Bonds, which would be paid through the Central, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and National Products Banks, the remaining bonds, together with accrued interest, would be paid by the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. Payment would be made in national currency regardless of location. He requested that the supervisors inspect the lottery tickets and the ticket stubs to facilitate the lottery drawing.

Each drawn ticket was presented to the chairman for verification, and then to the supervisors for confirmation before the winning numbers were announced. Wu Chaoshu Discusses the Effectiveness of Boycotting Japanese Goods in the Resistance Against Japan 267

China's Economic Structure is Loosely Organized, Giving it Advantages over Japan in Wartime

Direct Negotiations with Japan are Not Impossible, but Impractical

Declines to Serve as Minister of Justice, Willing to Exert Effort in Matters Directly Related to the National Crisis

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited Mr. Wu Chaoshu, a member of the Central Executive Committee, this morning to discuss various issues. His detailed comments are recorded below:

Using Strengths to Overcome Weaknesses 268

According to Mr. Wu, in this current period, military affairs are of primary importance, followed by diplomacy. However, there is one weapon whose power and effectiveness is as important as military force, or even surpasses it. Unfortunately, it has not been used effectively. What is it? It is economics. China's economy lacks organization, but it still maintains its inherent rural socio-economic structure. Therefore, if a problem arises in one area, while other areas are inevitably affected, the overall situation will not be jeopardized. As such, when compared to Japan economically, China is actually superior and can maintain the spirit of individual economic independence. Japan's economy is a highly organized nation. Because of this organization, problems in one area often affect the entire situation. Therefore, China's lack of economic organization is a major drawback during peacetime, but it is now an advantage during this difficult time. In terms of military equipment, the gap between China and Japan is significant. However, in terms of economics, China's strengths offset Japan's weaknesses. The people of China should know themselves and their enemy, using their strengths to overcome the enemy's weaknesses. The method for this is to implement a boycott of Japanese goods and impose economic sanctions. The import of Japanese goods into China is as harmful as tanks and airplanes at Lu Fengkou and Shimenzhai. If the people of China advocate being the military's support, there is no other way to achieve this. This is far more effective than empty talk of saving the nation. Look at Germany's expulsion of Jews. Orders were issued and implemented immediately, with the whole nation in unison. Their spirit is admirable, due to their well-organized infrastructure. In China, it must be initiated voluntarily by the people to be effective. What is the point if the government leads, but the people remain indifferent? A friend of mine has not used Japanese goods for decades, for reasons I do not know, but if every Chinese person had this spirit, we could certainly bring Japan to its knees.

Direct Negotiations 269

As for direct negotiations, interactions between countries always involve direct negotiations. China and Japan can certainly engage in direct negotiations, but in the current situation between Japan and China, direct negotiations would require Japan to demand recognition of puppet organizations and various illegal demands. What negotiations would be possible then? In short, it is not that direct negotiations are not permissible, but that direct negotiations are not feasible. As for the progress of the League of Nations' advisory committee of twenty-two nations, it is still uncertain. The establishment of this committee is also dependent on the overall situation and how it evolves to determine the appropriate course of action.

Mandated Governance 270

Germany and the United States' request for Japan to return mandated governance of the South Seas Islands has become less prominent, but it will eventually be resolved. Currently, it seems to be only Germany and the United States involved. However, due to Australia's relationship with the South Seas, the United Kingdom will inevitably intervene in this matter. Germany is temporarily not actively pursuing this issue due to the severity of its anti-Jewish policies. Once the anti-Jewish issue is resolved, it will then resolve this problem. It is difficult to say what the outcome will be, but if Mussolini's Four-Power Pact succeeds, it will be easily resolved.

Declines to Serve as Minister of Justice 271

Furthermore, the Central government requested that I serve as the Minister of Justice. Although I heard this suggestion while in Beijing, I did not agree and have formally declined. Some may say that during this time of national crisis, everyone should join the effort. However, I am only willing to exert my effort in matters that are directly related to the national crisis. Additionally, I have already stated that I will not accept the position of Chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee when I attended the Foreign Affairs Committee previously. I only agreed to serve as interim chairman. Recently, some people have written to me, addressing me directly as Chairman of the Foreign Affairs Committee, which is a misunderstanding.

Advises Them to Persuade Fellow Businesses to Resolve Firmly

Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to banks and native banks, urging them to stop lending to treacherous merchants to facilitate the boycott of Japanese goods. The letter stated: "Regarding the fact that since the Shanghai ceasefire, Japanese aggression has intensified, the loss of territory has expanded, and the treacherous merchants who sell Japanese goods are becoming increasingly brazen, it is because the public lacks methods to restrain them, and so-called public opinion is not enough to move them. This chamber believes that to impose an economic blockade on the enemy, we must first impose an economic blockade on the treacherous merchants. Otherwise, it will be empty talk and only make us a laughingstock. We request that your association notify your members to investigate if any businesses that they have dealings with are secretly selling Japanese goods. Once such circumstances are discovered, they should immediately stop providing loans and recall any outstanding loans to warn the treacherous merchants. This is the most crucial task for saving the nation at present. We hope that you will sincerely persuade your fellow businesses to resolve firmly and diligently fulfill this task."

Municipal Government Investigates and Bans Inferior Coins 273

The Proliferation of Inferior Currency Hampers Social and Economic Development

Sends a Letter to the Jianghai Customs to Ban the Import of Inferior Coins

The Municipal Government received a letter from the Municipal Party Department, which forwarded a petition from the Fresh Pork Industry Association requesting an investigation and ban on inferior coins to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. It sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs requesting an investigation and ban on the import of inferior coins, and also instructed the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau to handle the matter. The Municipal Party Department's letter and the Fresh Pork Industry Association's petition are recorded below:

The Municipal Party Department's letter to the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Kuomintang stated: "Regarding the Fresh Pork Industry Association's petition stating that the market is flooded with inferior coins, causing significant losses to merchants and requesting strict enforcement to alleviate their difficulties, this is because the proliferation of inferior coins in the market is detrimental to social and economic development. If strict measures are not taken, the public will suffer greatly. We are forwarding the original petition for your review and action."

The Fresh Meat Industry's Petition: The Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association petitions the Municipal Party Department, stating that the market is flooded with inferior coins, causing significant losses to merchants, and requesting an investigation and ban by the government authorities to alleviate their difficulties. Our association has received reports from members such as Yuan Chunyuan and others, stating that since the government's decision to change to the yuan system, currency unification and convenient calculation have greatly benefited merchants and the public. However, the multitude and inconsistent quality of silver coins are causing even greater harm. The principle that bad money drives out good money is a well-established economic principle. The current proliferation of inferior coins and the gradual reduction of good subsidiary currency in this city proves the validity of this statement. There are numerous types of subsidiary currency circulating in this city, totaling no fewer than twenty or thirty kinds. The silver content varies, and the market prices are inconsistent. Among them, there is a type of Xiamen official silver dollar that is universally accepted in the market. However, wholesalers and native banks require significant discounts and premiums. Merchants earn a significant amount of silver coins every day, and the so-called Xiamen official silver dollars often account for 60% to 70% of their earnings. Native banks display exchange rates, of course, based on good subsidiary currency, such as exchanging 1,230 coins for one small silver dollar. However, if exchanging Xiamen official silver dollars for silver, it requires exchanging 1,270 coins for one hundred yuan. There is no distinction when merchants use these coins, but they often lose two or three yuan per hundred when exchanging them. Other coins such as Dalian, Changsha, New Nine-Year, Eleven-Year, Thick-Edged, and Big-Bellied coins have many names and inconsistent prices. Fellow businesses suffer losses when exchanging them. If calculated annually, the amount of this unnecessary loss is not small. Merchants have been suffering losses for years and are in great distress. Therefore, we are sending this letter to your association to request that you forward it to the government authorities to investigate and ban inferior coins to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. It seems that the current method should be to request the financial authorities to find a way to recover and recast these coins and to strictly investigate and ban their import to cut off their source. Once the source is cut off, inferior coins can be eliminated. Recovering and recasting coins can achieve a unified effect. Based on the report, we are preparing this document to be submitted to your association for review and to request that you forward it to the authorities to investigate and ban inferior coins to alleviate the merchants' difficulties for the public good.

Regarding the nature of this war and its combatants, let's listen to the confessions of the vanguard of imperialism:

To resist Soviet Russia, China and Japan must unite and communicate with Britain, America, Italy, and France to understand their methods so that it can succeed." | See the secret agreement between Japan and the puppet "China Federation" as reported in the March 29th edition of the Shen Bao.

This slogan has already been proclaimed not only in the Far East but throughout the world.

Seeing the success of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan, they become even more envious and want to launch a final, desperate attack. This is a fate determined by history and is unavoidable because a new era must emerge from the old shell. People living in the old era cannot survive in the new world because they breathe differently and will inevitably commit suicide in the old world. This is the greatest tragedy caused by human stupidity. But what can you do for someone who voluntarily commits suicide, no matter how much compassion you have? The greatest compassion is to fulfill their wishes as soon as possible. Therefore, from a historical perspective and from the perspective of imperialism itself, this world war is not meaningless. The nature of this war has changed and taken on new elements. Unlike the previous wars between imperialist powers, this war is an international war on the vertical axis but a war between 125 million oppressed slaves and their rulers fighting for freedom on the horizontal axis. Therefore, it deserves our special attention.

But which group do we belong to? We must think carefully to decide our fate in this war. The fact is that you cannot hide on the sidelines and watch the excitement.

From the secret agreement between Japan and the puppet regime, it seems that Japan is willing to serve as the vanguard. To achieve a greater effect, China has been sacrificed under the "convenient arrangements" of this vanguard. But the importance of this supporting role cannot be denied. Feeling nominally isolated, they have created a fictitious "Chinese Federation Empire" as a source of spiritual comfort, which shows the difficulty of being a vanguard and the painstaking efforts of the invaders.

All of this is nonsense. In the end, the real decision lies in which path we are willing to take.

In the past (and perhaps still today), our esteemed country was prostrating before the throne of European and American imperialism. "China is now in love with Geneva," which even a cunning old fox like Lytton could see. A few years ago, we even tried to "lead the way," but the powerful foreigners were too merciless. Not only did they not show compassion, but they kicked him out of Geneva. As a result, the dream of occupying a seat at the bottom of the "Loyalty Hall" was finally shattered. But the innate nature cannot be changed, so we look westward, wandering like an abandoned woman, creating the chaotic phenomenon of the past few years. If you ask which group we belong to in this world, our answer is "unclassifiable."

First, it is clear that we are not a capitalist country, although we are constantly flirting with imperialism. There is still a slogan of "overthrowing imperialism" in the "Legacy" and we are being fiercely oppressed. But we are definitely not a socialist country. We are working hard on the "bandit suppression" movement. So, it is difficult to say which group we belong to. We are neither part of imperialism nor good friends with socialism. How can we survive in this world? What group do we belong to?

The Severity of the Problem 279

— Bing

| Written to a friend named Ji Chou |

I have long wanted to write you this letter, but I do not know where you are now. At the edge of this world, I have been trampled into an abyss of ten thousand fathoms, and how did you encounter the same fate!

Lately, the goddess of spring has arrived in the world. Every morning, the sparse sunlight shines through the cracks in the east-facing window into my snail-sized living space. The thin bedding seems to ripple with warmth. Ah, the gifts of nature are still impartial. Afraid of wasting the grace of the sun, I excitedly jumped out of bed.

But it was at this moment that my feelings were triggered. The rich are still snuggling in warm beds, embracing women, dreaming of their paradise, because the times have favored them. Money is rolling around them. Another group is already starting their busy lives. To begin the day, the first thing is to hurry to the vegetable market with a bamboo basket, jostling and bustling, and who is not dreaming of ascending to heaven, building the foundation of personal comfort!

Having become a traitor to the masses, I cannot step into the circle of ordinary life. I can only recall: yesterday morning I didn't eat a sesame cake, and my stomach was very hungry. Today it is as normal as it should be! What does it matter! Even if there is no food for lunch or even dinner, what does it matter! Fundamentally speaking, in this society full of jackals and wolves, it is a blessing that we have not been devoured by them! I have recognized this, so every time I get hungry, I comfort myself this way.

But where is the problem?

I only want to say that there are so many things in this society that make us young people feel indignant and distressed. The surrounding environment, as reflected in our eyes, is a series of blows. Look, on that side, a group of people are using all kinds of vile tactics - flattery, arrogance, oppression, and sucking - to enjoy a life of luxury, consuming Lidu, living in high-rise buildings, not satisfied with the enjoyment, and constantly playing the game of harming others. On this side, a group of people are toiling and struggling all day long, but still freezing and starving, fully demonstrating the two vastly different worlds. This is such a hateful thing!

Look, the life of the entire nation is already in extreme danger. The loss of the Northeast, the humiliation of the Shanghai Incident, even if we don't talk about it, the Japanese warlords have blinded our authorities, who have no sense of national consciousness. Even more fiercely, they have occupied our Rehe. Although our country usually maintains an army of hundreds of thousands, they cannot resist a few hundred Japanese soldiers in battle. What is the reason? Is it really impossible to resist? Even a three-foot-tall child would not believe it, because of their own interests, because they are not determined to resist, so the Japanese soldiers can drive straight in, so our country has lost one province after another, so the nation is increasingly approaching the brink of destruction.

Are these not more serious than personal problems! As the ancient saying goes: "When the skin is gone, what will the hair cling to?" This has explained the meaning acutely.

Of course, pressing personal problems need to be solved urgently, but the key to this problem lies in the masses, in the entire nation. To solve personal problems, we must also solve the problems of the masses and the nation.

The wheels of time have crushed us into an abyss of ten thousand fathoms. Can we just let it crush us?

Just being pessimistic and negative is a sign of self-destruction. Rushing blindly is also useless. What we need is a kind of enzymatic strength. My friend, you are the backbone of our group. Although you have encountered the same fate, I am ashamed that I only have these feelings. Please give me a concrete answer!

Wish you well

Your brother Bing, March 22nd

"Character Bullet" Work (Continued) 280

— Xu Jie

The poet's heart is in his mouth, the prostitute's heart is in her genitals; simply because everyone regards the mouth as more precious than the genitals, they all worship the poet's heart and despise the prostitute's!

A lyric poet cannot speak of love without poetry, a prostitute cannot speak of love without sexual intercourse. Aren't these two kinds of love often expressed, but not true love?

What is the taste of love? The blood of a warrior and the tears of a prostitute, mixed with the semen of a man suffering from spermatorrhea!

The fallen leaves proudly think that autumn is called by them!

A manure cart overturned on the road. No crime, because it is impossible to tell whose manure it is!

A beautiful woman can kill not only men, but also women. If she comes to seduce her beloved husband.

Love is like eating melon seeds. When you don't want to eat them anymore, it's hard to let go.

When visiting a mountain, it often seems near but is actually far away, but sometimes when you objectively estimate it to be far, you arrive after just one turn. Perhaps this is the reason why love drives young people crazy!

A blind man: "I wish I weren't blind, even if I became deaf."

A deaf man: "I wish I weren't deaf, even if I became blind."

This is life!

Comparing a woman to a flower is the best analogy. When a gentle breeze brushes against her, she sways proudly, but when a strong wind comes, she silently submits.

The truth of deduction is nurtured, the truth of induction is collected, and the truth of dialectical clarification is fought for.

When a person is born, they create "their own world." In middle age, they create "their own children." In old age, they create "their own corpse." This is everyone's three-part creative work!

Railways are built for trains, roads are made for cars, and the sun is born for tall buildings!

The times are like ink. Without the ability to change the times, one first changes the pen tip. The color will not change!

People often say that trains are fast, but they don't know that their speed lies in the wheels!

The car body above the wheels forgets itself, as if it is flying!

There is no one who cherishes time less than the person who invented the clock, and also those who...

Page 23

A word... the creation is art... Song...? What is it to give birth to a living person?

The eyes are in front, so no critic can see his own back and heart.

Killing a criminal, the tens of thousands of innocent sperm in his body die!

A man's love is water, a woman's love is a cup: when the water is gone, the cup is just empty, but anyone can fill it; when the cup is broken? The water flows freely without a place to go!

Old playwright, this is your mirror: Late at night, the dog thinks it is very peaceful, walking steadily and wagging its tail while barking.

Love is like snow on the road. Once it melts, what's left is mud.

To those who move forward with the flowing water, the stationary grass is a kind of reverse current; this is also how the times and pioneers see people.

Shop Assistant Communications

A Gentleman Can Be Deceived With Propriety 281

Editor:

After reading Miss Jin's "Can Love Simultaneously Accommodate Several People?" in the Shop Assistant Communications, two thoughts are deeply imprinted in my mind. First, male and female employees should respect each other's personality when working together. Second, the emerging female profession should be protected.

I have also heard that Miss Jin, so-called the "Queen," is suffering spiritually, but her so-called spiritual suffering is here, not there.

Because her appearance is relatively good, it has attracted the attention of a few male colleagues. Some write love letters to tease her, some pursue her after closing time, and some tease her at ordinary times, clinging to her like flies to carrion. But she always treats them with indifference, like water or ice, ignoring them completely.

Sitting at home, disaster comes from the sky. Because their goals are difficult to achieve, they come up with various methods to destroy and slander her. Recently, they have also impersonated Miss Jin to submit articles to your esteemed publication, in order to damage Miss Jin's reputation. At the same time, they also use the power of your esteemed publication to make the manager understand the misconduct of male and female colleagues, change the policy, and hope to reach the point of destroying the female profession. Their treacherous intentions can be seen from this.

Editor: A woman who doesn't even have the ability to choose a man, let alone judgment, cannot speak of the sanctity of love, let alone the female profession.

"I want bear's paw, and I also want fish." These two sentences insult women to the extreme. I wonder what Miss Jin, the real one, would think when she sees them.

I am an old colleague who has worked in the XX National Goods Company for more than ten years, and also a magistrate with children. I can no longer speak of love, let alone acidic reactions. However, for the sake of the future of the female profession, I have no choice but to speak out righteously. Please teach me, sir. If you think it still contains other motives, you might as well come to our company to investigate. I, Ge Zai, write again.

X X X X X

Editor's note: After reading Mr. Ge's letter, we learned that the letter from Miss Jin that we published the day before yesterday was fabricated by her male colleagues. Moreover, the motive for fabricating this letter is extremely despicable. Here, we cannot help but express our deepest apologies to Miss Jin and Mr. Ge. We dare not hide our mistakes; therefore, today we specially publish Mr. Ge's letter here, hoping that people in society and the manager of Miss Jin's store will understand this fact and not fall for the tricks of this group of good-for-nothings.

It has been more than three months since this column was born. Looking back on these three months, we have tried our best to answer the questions of the shop assistants with all our wisdom and sincerity. We originally hoped to use this very meager power to relieve the pain of the shop assistants to some extent. Everyone who reads our communications every day can probably understand this spirit of serving society! Unexpectedly, "a gentleman can be deceived with propriety." Our good intentions have actually been used by these people, which is really heartbreaking to say. Finally, we have no choice but to borrow Mr. Ge's tone and shout loudly: I hope people in society will cherish this column that serves society.

Fiction

Time in a Dream (Continuation of Twenty-One) 282

— Qin Shouou

Number sixteen was the last house in the alley, an Italian country-style building with a garden full of flowers. At the same time, someone was playing the piano inside the house. The bright and beautiful piano sound lightly crossed the half-closed gauze window and floated out leisurely, making Wu Yi stand outside the door, enjoying it freely, and he was too lazy to reach out and ring the doorbell.

"Old Wu! Why don't you go in?" Yu Lin happened to be coming back from outside, so he used the briefcase he was carrying in his hand to bump hard into Wu Yi, who was listening to the piano sound with all his attention.

"Ah! This piano is played so well..." Wu Yi praised as he followed Yu Lin into the house. At that time, the piano sound had stopped.

"Probably his wife is playing it!" Yu Lin walked in front, used the key to open the spring lock on the door, then turned sideways and let Wu Yi go in first.

Next to a large black piano stood a woman in a light green dress. She was petite, with a slightly round face, scarlet lips, and lively and bright eyes, clearly showing her extraordinary health and beauty.

"This is my wife, this is Old Wu! Haha! It's very interesting, Old Wu, you're seeing your matchmaker for the first time! Shouldn't you say thank you?" Yu Lin dropped the briefcase in his hand and lay down on a sofa, laughing excitedly.

Indeed, this was a very strange thing! Although Wu Yi and Yu Lin were the closest of old friends, he had never met his wife before today. The reason was not so abnormal, because when Wu Yi had just returned to the country, Ms. Mao Jufen was giving birth. After giving birth, she suffered a very serious illness and rested in the hospital for more than a year. Therefore, although she was the sole introducer of Wu Yi and Ms. Liu Suzhen's marriage, she was absent twice due to illness during the engagement and wedding. After she recovered from her illness, she had visited Wu Yi's residence several times, but she always went in the morning, when Wu Yi was sound asleep, so of course they couldn't meet. In the middle, she went to Tianjin for six or seven months to visit her aunt. With these three reasons, Wu Yi and her were like playing hide-and-seek, always missing each other.

"Sister-in-law!" Wu Yi first greeted her respectfully, according to custom.

"Ah! Mr. Wu, I often wanted to see you, but it was always not coincidental! It's so interesting that we only met today!" Although Ms. Mao was already a mother who had given birth to a child, her age was only twenty-four, much younger than Wu Yi and Yu Lin. Therefore, she still fully retained her innocence, spoke more crisply than Yu Lin, and her attitude was of course more generous than every woman.

Wu Yi also felt that this meeting today was very peculiar and interesting, and a satisfied smile appeared on his face. "Mr. Wu! The 'Sweet, Sour, Bitter, and Spicy' section you write in the Star Daily is really both humorous and profound. I really don't know how you come up with it!" Ms. Mao leaned on a swivel chair next to Wu Yi's seat and expressed her admiration to him very warmly, as if they were old friends who had been separated for many years, and once they met, they had endless words to pour out. "I heard Sister Suzhen say that you put a lot of thought into it and often put down your bowl suddenly while eating; indeed, writing is very hard, and it's even harder to write well. People who read it think it's interesting, but they never know how much effort the writer puts in!"
